German Industry Inspection Group Arrives in Guangzhou

Guangzhou Correspondence: When Sun Ke, Minister of Railways, previously visited Germany, he contacted the German industry group and welcomed German industrialists to invest in China and develop various Chinese industries to seek cooperation between the economic circles of China and Germany. At that time, the German Industrial Association agreed to organize an inspection group to come to China to conduct an initial investigation of the economic and industrial situation in southern and northern China. Then, they would return to Germany to formulate a development plan, negotiate with each other, and then invest. In February of this year, the German Industry Inspection Group was established and set out for China on the Japanese mail ship Hakone Maru from the Port of Marseille on February 28. The Ministry of Railways sent Counselor Jin Jingui to welcome them. The ship arrived in Hong Kong at 9 a.m. on March 30. The members of the group stayed overnight at the Kowloon Island Hotel. On the morning of the 31st, they took a ship from Hong Kong to Guangzhou and arrived in the province at 1:30 p.m. The German consul and all the German expatriates in Guangzhou went to the port to welcome them. The provincial government sent representative Jiang, the municipal government sent representative Liang, and representatives from the provincial and municipal party departments and various chambers of commerce were also present to greet them. The German industry group consisted of a total of twelve people, including eight members and the rest being interpreters and attendants. The members of the group and their brief resumes are investigated as follows: (1) Head of the group, Heunich Ketgnann, 57 years old, has served as the manager, director, and representative of the board of directors of the Firma Heine A.G. Leipzig factory. He is currently the leader of the German Industrial Association, Chairman of the Saxon Industrial Association, and a member of the German Industrial Association. (2) German industrial representative, engineer and Doctor of Philosophy H.C. Carl Wendt, 55 years old, has served as the factory manager, office director, and chairman of the German Engineering Society of the Krupp factory. (3) German electrical industry representative, Professor of Industrial University Prot. Dettmar Hannover, has worked on the design of the Soviet government's electricity industry construction and has written extensively. (4) Civil engineering industry representative Rademacher, 51 years old, is currently a senior architect of the German Railway Bureau. The Die Anatolische Eisenbahn of the German Asia Minor Railway was operated by him. He also participated in the construction of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway in China and is quite familiar with the Chinese situation. He is also good at banking and has worked in the Deutsche Bank. (5) German machine industry representative Direktor Von Gontard, 59 years old, has served as a construction engineer and worked for many years at the Firma Hensohel S. Sohn A.G. in Kassel factory and served as a director. (6) Financial advisor to the industry inspection group Dr. Jer Gacody has served as a lawyer for the Great Wall and National Bank International-Bank and has worked in major banks in Paris and London. He has considerable experience in Chinese economy. (7) Representative of the Central Bank, Dr. Schipprl, has served as a counselor of the German Ministry of Finance and a bank director. His main purpose in coming to China is to investigate China's financial and economic situation and China's currency reform. (8) M. Th. Strewe, Secretary of the Industry Inspection Group. After the group arrived, they were invited by the provincial and municipal governments to rest briefly at the New Asia Hotel in Xihai Kou, and then had lunch. At 3:30 p.m., Chen personally received them in the foreign flower hall, and the guests and hosts had a pleasant conversation. After the tea party, photos were taken, and they left at 4:00 p.m. At 4:20 p.m., they went to the municipal government. Mayor Lin Yungai happened to be heading north and had not returned, so the municipal government secretary received them on his behalf and held a tea party to welcome them. They left after 6:00 p.m. In the evening, the provincial government held a banquet in the foreign flower hall to welcome them. The banquet started at 7:00 p.m., and the heads of various agencies accompanied them, totaling more than 80 people, divided into eight tables. During the banquet, Chen Mingshu delivered a welcoming speech, and the head of the inspection group replied. Toasts were exchanged, and the banquet dispersed around 10:00 p.m. Tonight (April 1), the municipal government will hold a formal welcome meeting to entertain the members of the group. During the day, they will visit the Huanghuagang Mausoleum of the 72 Martyrs, Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall, and Guanyin Mountain Park. On the 2nd, they will visit Luogang Cave. On the 3rd, they will inspect the province's construction projects and then discuss cooperation methods with the Construction Department. After the matter is completed, they will leave Guangzhou on the 4th, take the German ship Derfllirgesr from Hong Kong to Shanghai, and then go to Beijing, Hankou, Beiping, and the three northeastern provinces. After completing inspections in various places, a specific plan will be published. (April 1)

Guangzhou National Goods Movement Parade

Guangzhou Correspondence: On the first of this month, all circles in Guangzhou held a grand meeting to promote the National Goods Movement. The meeting place was located at the East Drill Ground. A huge archway was built outside the field, with the words "National Goods Promotion Meeting" written on it. In the center was the meeting stage, with four loudspeakers installed in front of the stage. The front of the stage was the command stage, the front of the stage was the gathering place for students from various schools, the north was the gathering place for party and government agencies and various groups, the south was the gathering place for national goods parade costume teams and various labor unions, and the west was the gathering place for naval, land, military police. Around the field, there were boy scouts and military police maintaining order. After 10 a.m., members of various groups and staff of various agencies arrived one after another. The meeting started at 12 noon. The party committees of the province and municipality, the provincial and municipal governments, the Department of Construction, the General Chamber of Commerce, the Provincial Business Federation, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Overseas Comrades Society, the Machinery Industry Association, the General Labor Union, the Labor Union Federation, the Women's Federation, the Women's Rights Movement Association, the Provincial Women's Association, the Seamen's Union, and the Police Alumni Association were the presidium, with a total of eighteen groups. Liu Fenqiao, a member of the Municipal Party Committee, was publicly elected as the chairman of the presidium. After the ceremony, Luo Weijiang, executive member of the Provincial Party Committee, announced the reasons for the meeting, saying that unemployment is increasing day by day, social unrest is due to the increase in unemployment, and politics is not stable. However, upon closer examination of why the people's livelihood is in such a predicament, on the one hand, it is due to the constraints of unequal treaties and economic oppression, and at the same time, it is also due to our people's unwillingness to use national goods. In recent years, China has become a sales market for imperialist goods. Since our country's economic power is controlled by foreigners, is it not empty talk to talk about overthrowing imperialism? In the future, we must implement the overthrow of imperialist aggression and save the nation from danger, and we must promote national goods to remedy the leaks. If national goods are revitalized, productivity will naturally increase, foreign goods will naturally decrease imports, and money will not flow out, and the people's livelihood can be maintained. If the people's livelihood is stable, then the society and politics will naturally become more peaceful, and disasters can also be reduced. Next, representatives of the Provincial Government Deng Hua, representatives of the Municipal Party Committee Pu Liangzhu, representatives of the Eighth Route Army Feng Luanhuang, and representatives of the General Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, and the Women's Rights Association delivered speeches in turn. The meaning of promoting national goods was fully expressed. After the speeches, the following proposals were put forward by the presidium of the conference: (1) The government should establish a national goods bank, a national goods exhibition, a national goods sales market, and a daily necessities factory. (2) Please the Central Party Department and the National Government to strictly order all agencies, groups, and schools to use national goods, and those who violate the order will be severely punished. (3) Please the provincial and municipal party committees to be responsible for convening all circles to organize the Guangdong National Goods Promotion Association. (4) Please the Central Government to implement incentives for the production of national goods. (5) Please the government to guarantee the patent rights of various national goods inventions. (6) Notify all silk weaving companies across the country not to use foreign artificial silk raw materials to weave and pretend to be domestic silk. The above proposals were immediately voted on by the whole field, and then high-definition photos were taken, slogans were shouted, and music was played and the meeting was dismissed. It was already 1 p.m. The various circles immediately formed a team to parade, led by Wang Renrong, deputy chief of the headquarters adjutant's office, riding a horse as a guide, followed by the Party and National Flag, the General Assembly Parade Flag, the headquarters military band, and the municipal party boy scouts. The parade team was divided into four major teams, and each major team was divided into several sub-teams, totaling about 100,000 people. There were various styles of parade items, everything that should be there, totaling from the East Drill Ground, passing through Hui Ai East Road, Yong Han South Road, Tianzi Wharf, the Bund, Xihai Kou, Liu Ersan Road, Cailan Street, Fude Road, Shibaba, Shiqifu, Yang Lane, Shangjiupu, Xiguayuan, Fengning Road, Ximenkou, Hui Ai West Road, to sign and disperse in front of Central Park. It was already 3:30 p.m. Looking at the national goods costume team that paraded that day, there were no less than 50 teams. Among them, a large homemade coconut broom with the words "Sweep Away Imported Goods" written on it was particularly meaningful. (March 1 evening)

The Great Genghis Khan Festival

Inner and Outer Mongolian Princes Participate Together

The Form of the Mausoleum and Its Arrangement

Suiyuan Correspondence: When we browse through the Yuan Dynasty chronicles, the one who opened up the glory of Eastern land warfare history and established the mighty power of the Yellow race should be Genghis Khan. It has been more than 800 years since then. European war historians still praise him endlessly, calling him the hero of the Yellow race. Although the hero is gone, the mausoleum still exists. The tomb of Genghis Khan is located in the Jungar Banner of the Yikezhao League in Inner Mongolia. A grand festival is held every year on the 15th and 16th of April. The princes of various leagues and banners in Inner and Outer Mongolia gather at that time. It is extremely grand. Now that the festival is approaching, the princes of various leagues and banners have sent envoys to the Suiyuan and Baotou areas to prepare sacrificial offerings. The mausoleum is surrounded by 250 miles, with 500 households living there, called the Outer Guard, specializing in guarding the mausoleum. Each year, in addition to the products within the 250 miles being received by them, the remaining shortfall is subsidized by the leagues and banners, which has evolved into a hereditary system for hundreds of years. Except for the 500 households, no other leagues or banners can live there. Those close to the mausoleum are the Inner Guard, specializing in guarding the mausoleum all night, burning incense and dusting. The monthly income is slightly higher than that of the Outer Guard. Both the Inner and Outer Guards belong to the "Jinu" (Mongolian for mausoleum official). The position of "Jinu" is quite solemn and is concurrently held by the leader of the Yikezhao League. The form and arrangement of the mausoleum are very different from those of the Ming and Qing mausoleums. It was not a burial in the ground. It is a small silver box, three feet five inches long, and one foot five inches wide and high, placed on a mica stone table, with a large offering table in front, on which sacrificial offerings are placed. The incense burner is one foot five inches high, the candlestick is two feet five inches high, and there are many other sacrificial offerings, all made of silver, stored separately and only taken out during the festival. This three-foot silver box is quite luxuriously made, impervious to wind and rain, and difficult to erode by water and soil. It is a pity that it is placed inside a felt tent, which is not very elegant (what is called Mongolian style in the local language). This felt tent is replaced every twelve years, costing more than 2,500 yuan. It is different from ordinary felt tents and is larger and extremely strong. The interior can accommodate 150 people, and incense smoke lingers all day, creating a solemn atmosphere. Whether on foot or on horseback, when passing by the mausoleum, they all pay respects. When the festival arrives, it is extremely lively, with iron cavalry in groups, camel teams traveling thousands of miles, the sound of reed pipes echoing throughout the land, and the voices of people clamoring. Red men and green women, white-haired old men and yellow-haired children, ride on fine horses and rush to the scene. The reporter intends to visit Jungar Banner on this day to pay homage to the outstanding figures of the East, and I will surely gain something in terms of news materials. (March 24)

Relief for Shipping and Transportation at the Zhenjiang Estuary

The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau is Considering Two Measures. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly petitioned the Ministry of Railways because the Zhenjiang Estuary Station's connection with ships is hampered by silting and rising tides in the river channel during autumn and winter, causing significant losses to commerce and transportation. They requested the Bureau to extend the Zhenjiang Estuary Station to the customs house to facilitate transportation. On the 26th of last month, Liu Weichi, the Director of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau, led engineers to Zhenjiang and, together with committee members Lu and Hu from the Chamber of Commerce, surveyed the terrain. The Bureau believes that extending the Zhenjiang Estuary Station to the Zhenjiang Customs House is not a fundamental solution, as even if the station is extended to the Customs House, the river channel in front of the Customs House, although dredged, may soon lose its effectiveness. Therefore, the Bureau does not agree with this proposal. According to the Bureau's opinion, two measures are proposed: the first is to extend the railway line from Gaozi to the Zhenjiang Estuary to facilitate river transportation; the second is to extend the South Gate Station to the vicinity of the Dongfang Paper Mill at Beigushan. The cost of this project is estimated to be 300,000 to 400,000 yuan. Committee members Lu and Hu from the Chamber of Commerce are deeply concerned that the Bureau will adopt the first plan because Gaozi is too far from the old city, and Zhenjiang will find it difficult to benefit in the future. Therefore, they strongly advocate adopting the second plan. As for the required funding of 300,000 to 400,000 yuan, the Bureau suggests that the local government should raise the funds first, lend them to the Bureau, and be guaranteed by the Bureau's Silver Company, with the Bureau repaying the funds in installments over the years.

Hangzhou Express News

The Provincial Government previously received a proposal from the Department of Construction regarding whether Dahua Shipping Company should be granted an exclusive five-year operating permit on the Hangzhou-Changshan and Hangzhou-Weiping routes to guarantee their investment in hydrofoil boats. The Provincial Committee has now resolved to grant an exclusive operating permit for a term of ten years to encourage investment. The price of rice in Hangzhou has soared, with top-quality rice reaching 16.2 yuan per shi (unit of dry measure) and ordinary rice 13.6 yuan per shi. Ten days ago, there were rumors that desperate citizens were plotting to cause trouble for rice shops in Lake Side, intending to plunder them. Fortunately, Police Chief Li, acting on reports, took strict precautions, and the threat has dissipated invisibly for a week. However, the people's livelihood is becoming increasingly difficult, and it is hoped that the authorities will find a way to stabilize rice prices to maintain order. The Hangzhou General Chamber of Commerce, the Money Trade Association, and various banks were ordered to nominate members to the Public Bond Fund Management Committee. They separately nominated Xie Hucheng, Wang Ziqiu, and Xu Shucen as members. Now, they have been ordered to add one more member each to show transparency, as the rules for managing the funds have been revised. It is said that the Chamber of Commerce plans to nominate Yao Yinsheng, the Money Trade Association Li Chunzhi, and the banking industry Wang Xiangquan. The new tea from Mingqian in Xihu Beishan, Longjing, and other places has already been on the market, with prices ranging from 8 yuan per jin (unit of weight) to 10 or 12 yuan for finer varieties. Unfortunately, production is limited, totaling less than 100 jin. Tea merchants from various regions have already arrived in Hangzhou to purchase the tea.

Local Correspondence

Kunshan

Military and Police Suppression of Bandits in Yangcheng Lake. Yang Santai Temple in Yangcheng Lake, under the jurisdiction of Kunshan County, was occupied by bandits. The First Battalion of the 28th Regiment of the stationed army, together with Patrol Boat No. 20 of the Provincial Water Police 12th Squad, advanced by steamboat on the 3rd. The bandits had already fled. The military and police then burned the temple and patrolled the lake. At 2 p.m., in Yangcheng Lake Village, under the jurisdiction of Wuxian County, they suddenly encountered 30 to 40 bandit boats with over 300 bandits occupying the village. Upon seeing the government troops, they immediately opened fire and fired several cannons. After half an hour, the bandits were unable to resist and fled westward. In this operation, one bandit boat was captured. A police officer, Tang Lianquan, of the Water Police Vanguard Boat, was killed in action. Fierce Battle Between Soldiers and Bandits in Chenmu. At 2 p.m. on the 4th, 36 bandit boats with over 300 bandits arrived at Sharenba in Chenmu Town. The bandits had previously sent a letter to the town demanding 50,000 yuan, causing panic among all the shops and residents. Upon seeing the bandit boats arrive, their fear increased. Upon learning this, District Chief Dai Zuwei telegraphed the County Government, "At this time, the County Government was holding an anti-bandit meeting." County Chief Pang immediately consulted with Regiment Commander Yao and ordered Chen, the company commander of the First Company of the First Battalion stationed in Jiaozhi, to rush to suppress the bandits. Upon receiving the order, Company Commander Chen led his entire company of soldiers from Jiaozhi by steamboat. At 5 p.m., they arrived at the location and encountered the bandits. The two sides engaged in a fierce battle for about an hour. The bandits were unable to resist and retreated. In this operation, over ten bandits were killed, seven bandit boats were captured, and two hostages from Zhitang were rescued. The army suffered no casualties. The army is now temporarily stationed in Chenmu Town.

Qingpu

Military and Police Join Forces to Suppress Lake Bandits. After a large number of lake bandits were discovered at the Guanwang Temple, three miles from Zhujiajiao, the situation in Zhujiajiao Town became dangerous, with several alarms every night. After receiving the report, the County Government immediately ordered the County Police Force to join forces with the Water Police to pursue and suppress the bandits. It also ordered the land and water police force stationed in Jintan to attack from the right. It also telegraphed the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to request reinforcements. The previous day, an infantry company of the army was dispatched from Shanghai to attack from the front. After about four hours of fierce fighting, using machine guns and cannons, the bandits were unable to resist and fled in disarray toward the east, west, south, and Miaohu Lake. In this operation, over ten lake bandits were killed, one bandit boat was seized, and two hostages were rescued. Yang Jinbiao, a patrol officer of the First Squad of the Water Police, was injured in the head and legs and was immediately sent to the hospital for treatment. The military and police are still organizing forces to pursue and suppress the bandits. A Bride Disappears Before Her Wedding. Zou A’yun, a villager from the Mawangjing Township of Qingpu, engaged A’shi, the second daughter of Zhou Jinru from Zhoujia Village, as his wife through a matchmaker in the 15th year of the Republic. Last month, he notified the Zhou family that he had chosen an auspicious date ("the third day") for the wedding. Zhou also expressed his agreement. Zou made preparations for the wedding in advance and was extremely busy. The day before the wedding, relatives and friends gathered, a lavish banquet was prepared, and a bridal sedan was hired to go to the bride's house for the wedding. However, there was no movement at the Zhou's house. The sedan porters carried the bridal sedan back to the groom and inquired about the situation. He immediately went to the bride's house with the matchmaker to demand an explanation. Zou's father-in-law said that his daughter had disappeared the day before and asked for a postponement of the wedding. Zou believed that since the announcement had been made in advance and the change occurred so suddenly, there must be another reason, and he planned to file a lawsuit immediately. The matter is currently under mediation by relatives and friends, and it is not known how it will be resolved.

Suzhou

Arrest of Suspects Hiding Firearms. Sergeant Yan of the Fourth Precinct, acting on a report received at around 8 p.m. on the 5th, that several armed criminals were hiding in Fuxing Lane, Xinmin Bridge, led four officers to search the area. They arrested three suspects, including Yao Gouda, Wang Li Shi, and Zhang Li Shi. They also found three Browning pistols and ninety-three bullets. They were immediately taken to the precinct. According to Yao Gouda, he is from Changzhou and came to Suzhou on the 28th of last month. The pistols were sent to him by Wang Mingting, an acquaintance. Wang Li Shi and Zhang Li Shi corroborated the statement. That night, they were sent to the precinct office and then transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation on the 6th. Two Murders Occur in Suzhou Rural Areas. Wu A’quan, a villager from the foot of Hewan Mountain in Huguan, Suzhou Rural Area, was previously convicted of theft and sentenced to twelve years in prison. He was released last year after serving his sentence and lived an honest life as a farmer in his village. However, Yu A’yun, a villager from the same village, suspected Wu of stealing his property and killed him with a pig-slaughtering knife. Wu's family member, Wu Genshan, learned of the incident and reported it to the Public Security Bureau. The Public Security Bureau arrested Yu, and the local court confirmed that the death was caused by knife wounds. Yu A’yun was then taken to the court for interrogation and detention. In Pujia Village, Mudu Township, a man around thirty years old with knife wounds was found some days ago. His condition was critical. The Public Security Bureau immediately sent for a doctor to treat him, but it was too late to save him. The local court also confirmed that he had been murdered. The local authorities were ordered to provide a coffin for burial and to vigorously pursue the murderer.

Therefore, a special martial law order was issued, prohibiting people from traveling after 9 p.m. Meanwhile, the County Public Security Bureau increased the number of patrols and strengthened the defense of the city gates. Wuxi

Escalation of Dispute in Hat and Shoe Industry. A dispute between labor and management in the hat and shoe industry in this county has been prolonged without resolution. Recently, the Labor Organization Committee reported that Tang Zixuan, the owner of Yuxingxiang Store, was suspected of instigating the store's worker, Cai Xifu, to refuse to pay membership fees. The Executive Committee of the Labor Union, including Pan Yueting and Pan Laosi, reported this. The Public Security Bureau was requested to summon Cai Xifu for investigation. Guo Zirong also submitted a report to the County Government, accusing Pan Yueting and Pan Laosi of forcing workers to join the union. In the afternoon of the day before yesterday, Magistrate Sun summoned both parties to the case for questioning. As a result, Guo Zirong did not admit to paying monthly membership fees of thirty cents, claiming that he had not joined the union and had no obligation to pay membership fees. Magistrate Sun ordered Guo Zirong, Pan Yueting, and Tang Zixuan to be placed under police custody pending further investigation. Pan Yueting was subsequently released on bail by the Labor Organization Committee, and Guo Zirong and Tang Zixuan were also released on bail by their industry peers. Yesterday, the shop owners sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting them to forward a letter to the County Government, asking for the reasons for detaining Guo Zirong and others. Bao Xingyin Lured and Kidnapped by Bandits. Xingyin, the adopted daughter-in-law of Bao A’ren and Bao Zhou Shi, who are tenants near Kuatang Bridge outside the South Gate, is 19 years old and not yet fully developed. At the end of last month, she went to visit relatives in Nanqiao and was abducted by two bandits, Jiang Laowu and Xu Bingshan (both from Jiangbei), who took her to their home, dressed her in male attire to disguise her identity. Xu Bingshan also attempted to rape her twice, but Xingyin refused to undress, thus remaining chaste. On the night of the 5th of this month, Jiang and Xu led Xingyin to the railway station, intending to abduct her to Shanghai and sell her. They were discovered by railway police officers, who arrested Jiang, Xu, and Xingyin and brought them to the county for questioning. Xingyin confessed as described above, while the two bandits were evasive. Judge Zhou ordered the two bandits to be detained and released Xingyin to her parents-in-law to take home. Series of Robberies Occur in Jingyun Town. Over twenty households in the vicinity of Houyangfang in Jingyun Town, under the jurisdiction of the county, are lined up closely together and are considered well-off. Unexpectedly, around 11 p.m. the day before yesterday, eight or nine bandits speaking a strong northern accent, wearing short clothes, and armed with pistols, wooden sticks, flashlights, and other weapons arrived in the village. They first broke into the home of Feng Heshang and carried out a thorough robbery. They then proceeded to rob neighboring houses on both sides for about an hour before leaving with their loot. In this operation, three or four families were robbed, with total losses estimated at over 5,000 yuan. Use of Counterfeit Money Exposed and Suspect Apprehended. The Yanlingtang herbal medicine shop in Chenshe Town, Huaihai Township, was visited by Dai Jinkui the afternoon before yesterday.

He bought western ginseng, costing seven jiao, and paid with a five-yuan counterfeit banknote from the bank, receiving four yuan and three jiao in change. Later, the counterfeit was discovered and reported to the town's security corps, which tracked down and arrested Dai. Seven more counterfeit banknotes of the same kind were found on his person. Under interrogation, Dai Jinkui admitted to using counterfeit banknotes without hesitation. He was sent to the county yesterday for questioning. Penalty Imposed on Rafts Smuggling Taxable Goods. Sun Jinda, Wu Lanxuan, and others, residents of Shuanghe Town, Kaiyuan Township, Xixi County, recently purchased light bamboo and water bamboo from Anji County, Zhejiang Province, and transported them back to Wuxi by rafts. While passing through the Huangbudun Tax Card Special Tax Sub-Bureau, the bureau discovered that most of the bamboo rafts contained mixed bamboo, with light bamboo and water bamboo accounting for only three-tenths, worth about 14,000 yuan. The due tax was 280 yuan. After a long dispute, Sun and others only agreed to donate 100 yuan. The bureau then ordered the local guarantor, Sun Yizhen, to guard the bamboo rafts and requested the County Government to investigate the matter. County Chief Sun sent police to summon Sun Jinda for questioning. Lu, from the Second Section, interrogated him and ruled that Sun Jinda and others had included mixed bamboo in the rafts with the intention of cheating. According to regulations, they were ordered to pay 360 yuan in regular and additional taxes within two days to increase tax revenue. County Government Strictly Investigating Counter-Revolutionaries. The Wuxi County Government has continuously received confidential reports in recent days that a large number of counter-revolutionaries are hiding inside and outside the city, intending to incite unrest and engage in subversive activities. A small red triangular flag seized was kept on file, with the words "Armed Support for Workers and Peasants" written on it, and a sickle and an axe were drawn on it. Upon receiving the report, County Chief Sun secretly ordered the County Public Security Bureau, the police force, and political police to take strict precautions to maintain public order.

Winter Grain Collection Deadline Extended by One Month. The collection of money and grain in Wu County has been discussed in various townships. This winter grain collection was supposed to be completed by March 15th. However, the Financial Bureau has only collected 30-40%, which is unprecedented in recent years. The reason is that last year's famine left people with little savings. Moreover, since the implementation of the district system and the order to abolish the Baobao system, the original discussion regulations have been misunderstood by the villagers, leading them to wait and see. The Financial Bureau has now received approval from the Department of Finance to extend the deadline by one month to fully complete the collection. Yesterday (the 5th), a telegram was sent to urge supervisors in various districts to handle the matter.

Second Division of the Second District Dissatisfied with House Demolition for Road Construction. Sergeant Lu Released from Wujin. Xu Guangye, the former head of the Qianzhou Township Security Corps, caused a dispute over the arrest of the monk Ren Qinghuai of the Puji Temple. Lu Demao, a sergeant from the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, has been released. Yesterday, he reported to the headquarters that he had been suppressing the riot at Huangcun on March 27th when the thugs kidnapped Xu Guangye, the head of the Qianzhou Township Security Corps, and took him to the Wujin County Court. After the hearing, Lu was found to be not involved and was released. Xu was reportedly still under investigation for extortion and was being held in custody. Director Zhang reported this to Magistrate Shen for handling.

Jiashan

Kidnapping in Dongxiang. Yesterday night, two bandit boats suddenly arrived at the home of Li Fusheng, a farmer in Qitangtou, Yuhui, Dongxiang. The ten or so bandits were all armed with box cannons. They broke down the door and demanded money. When their demands were not met, they kidnapped the head of the household and his son, Da Yuan, demanding a ransom of 5,000 yuan for each person, to be paid within five days. Crackdown on Shipping. Since the Shanghai-Huzhou ships were converted to higher horsepower engines, their speed has increased, and the dikes of the villages of Yunjun, Shugen, and others under the jurisdiction of the county have been damaged. The County Government has been petitioned repeatedly to crack down on this, but with no results. Now that Magistrate Shen has taken office, the village associations have again petitioned to ban the ships.

Setting Up Public Night Schools. Lu Mengxiu, Director of the Education Bureau of Jiashan County, believes that enlightening the public is extremely important during the period of political tutelage. Therefore, he has included the establishment of ten public night schools in the county's education plan for this year, to be set up in both urban and rural areas, recruiting illiterate adults and teaching them common literacy, party doctrines, and abacus skills. He has drafted an implementation plan, purchased books and supplies, appointed principals, and begun early enrollment. The schools are scheduled to open uniformly on April 10th. Public Security Bureau Reassigns Large Number of Patrol Leaders. Because Lu Hong, the patrol leader of the Hongjiatan outpost, neglected his duties and violated police regulations, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau dismissed him. Hu Jun, the patrol leader of Patrol Boat No. 2 of the bureau, will fill the vacancy. Xu Gao, an investigator from the bureau, will fill the vacated patrol leader position. Wang Hao, the patrol leader of the Yaozhuang Bridge outpost, was approved to resign, and Cao Peng, a messenger from the bureau, will fill the vacated position. Wu Nishan, the patrol leader of the Third Outpost of the bureau, will be transferred to fill the vacated messenger position. Zhang Hanjie will fill the vacated patrol leader position of the Third Outpost. The relevant patrol officers have been notified accordingly.

Second Section of the Xiao-Chang Road Surveyed. Since the first section of the Xiao-Chang Railway, from Xiaoshan to Zhuji, began construction last month, a portion of the earthwork has been completed. It is now learned that the bureau has decided that the second section, from Zhuji to Yiwu, will also be built in two sections. The bureau has dispatched a survey team to begin surveying. Department Store Donation Bureau Accused of Extortion. The other night (the 2nd), the Yangfanqiao Department Store Donation Bureau outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan forcibly demanded a donation of ninety yuan from the owner of a night boat traveling from Daoxu, Shaoxing, to Xixing because it was carrying ten bales of cotton. The boat was allowed to sail only after the donation. Mr. Wang had no money, so the ten bales of cotton he was carrying were seized. Wang claimed that the cotton was purchased from Chejiapu and that a donation of four yuan had been made to the Shaoxing Cotton Donation Bureau at the time, and he had a donation ticket. Now that the bureau has seized the cotton, he went to Hangzhou to file a complaint with the Department of Finance on the 4th, accusing them of extortion. Special Report.

China Gradually Adopts the Gold Standard

Summary of the Draft Currency Law (3) (Continued)　　Abolition of Old Currency

The task of replacing the existing currency with the gold standard currency is entrusted to the National Currency System Commission, whose chairman is concurrently the Director of the Currency System Department. Provincial Currency System Commissions are also established as necessary to assist. The task of the Provincial Currency System Commissions particularly focuses on informing the public of the benefits of the new currency system, the penalties and restrictions on old currency, and the locations and official rates for exchanging old currency for new currency. 　　Abolition of Old Paper Currency　　The draft proposal by the Design Committee for reorganizing the Central Bank into the Central Reserve Bank stipulates that the issuance of paper currency should be exclusively handled by the new Central Reserve Bank in the plan. Therefore, this draft proposal seeks to recall the various paper currencies currently in circulation. When this draft becomes law, paper currencies issued by various provinces, localities, banks (except the Central Bank), shops, or private individuals should cease issuance and be withdrawn swiftly. The final recall date for paper currency in each province should not be earlier than the debt conversion date and should be announced at least one year in advance. Before this date, all paper currencies should be recalled at par value. However, if the paper currency depreciates excessively and remains so for a period, it is stipulated that it can be redeemed at a price lower than the face value under certain conditions, as determined by the Minister of Finance. 　　If a province, locality, provincial bank, or local bank cannot recall all its paper currency before the specified date, it must deposit sufficient gold standard currency in a designated agency and recall the circulating difference at par value. If sufficient currency is not available for this purpose, interest-bearing bonds can be used to withdraw the uncollected paper currency. 　　If a bank or other private organization has paper currency in circulation that cannot be fully recalled before the final recall date, a tax will be levied on the uncollected paper currency, at a rate of half a mill per month in the first year, one mill per month in the second year, and one and a half mills per month thereafter. Banks owing substantial amounts to the National Government are entitled to a reduction of three-quarters of the tax on the portion of their uncollected paper currency equal to their holdings of National Government bonds. After the bonds have been repaid by the government or sold by the bank, the tax-exempt portion of the paper currency must be reduced accordingly. Before the final recall date for paper currency, the government must settle its unfunded liabilities to banks with cash or various types of bonds.

Shortcomings of the Silver Standard Proposal

The Design Committee has studied the proposed plan to unify the national currency on a silver basis and then switch to a gold basis. According to the Committee's opinion, this proposal has significant errors for the following reasons: After the difficult task of unifying the currency system is completed, the desire to proceed with a gold basis and stipulate the necessary difference between the actual value and face value of silver coins will inevitably lead to an increase in the face value of silver coins. However, in the gold standard, the actual value of silver coins usually needs to be equal to two-thirds of the face value of silver coins. This method of relatively reducing domestic currency is indeed a painful move, which can make industry and export trade slump, harm the laboring class, and is extremely unfair to a certain class. If, in the future, credit gold standard currency is recast to replace the increased value of silver coins, the state must recall its newly issued silver standard currency and suffer a double loss, and it is also inconvenient for the people, which is unnecessary. 　　Moreover, proceeding with a gold-based plan using this indirect method means that the country continues to hold a second currency system reform. After the currency system is unified on a silver basis, a second reform based on gold must be carried out soon. This reform, in any case, is full of thorns, and if there is significant opposition during the second reform after the first reform has been completed, the move to adopt a gold basis will not be easily realized. 　　The indirect method also has a significant shortcoming, namely the loss of the huge seigniorage profit owned by the government. After the value of silver standard currency is increased to make it suitable for the gold standard, these currencies become credit currency, but the seigniorage profit that can belong to the government is dissipated into the hands of private individuals and no longer belongs to the government. These benefits are mostly obtained by speculators, who are most active during this period. The experience of the Straits Settlements in 1905 and 1906 due to the adoption of this currency system reform can provide us with a valuable lesson. 　　The indirect plan sooner or later requires huge loans to establish the necessary gold reserve. Conversely, the direct plan is truly self-sufficient except for the small amount of loans required at the beginning, and the loans can also be repaid with the profits obtained from the reform itself. The indirect plan also wastes time, making it impossible for China to enjoy the benefits of the gold standard enjoyed by almost all other important countries today after many years. 　　A unified gold standard currency is a major help to China's industry and commerce, which can increase production, develop foreign trade, and enhance the happiness of the people nationwide. The direct adoption of the gold standard method is also the most economical, has the least hindrance to domestic industry, and its greatest benefit is that it allows China to immediately adopt the gold standard in more advanced regions.

Second Match: Hong Kong Beats Shanghai　　…Result: 2 to 0　　Performance of the Two Teams Reaches Perfection　　Three Thousand Spectators Marvel at the Spectacle　　At 1 pm on the 6th, the second match of the Hong Kong and Shanghai teams for the volleyball championship was one of the most exciting scenes of the competition in a week. And the Hong Kong team also gradually progressed from then on, taking the lead with 6 to 4.

Turn the Tide, Shanghai Counterattacks

Seeing that the opponent was coming fiercely, the Shanghai team knew that it was not enough to resist without fighting hard, so they gathered their energy and worked hard to support. Surprise Victory, Hong Kong Succeeded

Hong Kong's repeated attacks were ineffective, so they changed their strategy and used the plan of flanking from both wings. The central army only took care of responding, and often entrusted the ball to both sides. The middle row of left and right wings then slammed the point where the ball landed, as fast as arrows, all in the left and right corners of the Shanghai side. Suddenly left and suddenly right, repeatedly hitting the key points. The Shanghai team was uncertain, taking care of this and losing that. It was really impossible for them to defend, and it was difficult to defend. Hong Kong was a smooth sailing, and had a winning momentum of 11 to 5.

Re-energize After Changing Positions

After changing positions, the Hong Kong team won victory after victory. Three serves added three more points. After this painful blow, the whole Shanghai team became more angry and worked together to strive forward. Sure enough, they also increased four points one after another, creating a situation of 14 to 9. The Women's Track and Field Championship: Harbin and Guangdong tied for first place.

For about seven minutes, there were still no points on the scoreboard. Later, Zhejiang got a free throw opportunity, and center Zhou Zuomin scored one point. Beiping saw Zhejiang taking the lead, and everyone perked up their spirits, bravely moving forward. Chen Shengkui scored repeatedly, and Wang Yuzeng also scored three times in a row, increasing the score frequently. Zhejiang then adjusted Yao Liang to be the left forward. Yao Liang was agile and scored two goals as soon as he joined. Beiping's Zhao Borong dribbled the ball and attacked, single-handedly driving straight in, but missed the shot. Wang Li, with his tall stature, patted the ball three times, and it rolled into the net. The result of the first half was 27 to 5, with Beiping winning.

Zhejiang Unable to Recover

In the second half, Zhejiang scored first again, but Beiping was unwilling to relax, using more aerial passes. Their tall stature gave them a lot of advantage. Zhejiang's passes were stagnant, and Wu Guolin's shots were quite accurate, but there was no teamwork, and his teammates could only sigh at the basket. After Zhao Borong of Beiping scored ten points in a row, their momentum was like adding fuel to the fire, unstoppable. The score increased with time. Zhejiang's formation gradually became chaotic, and morale wavered, leading to an irreversible situation. As a result, they lost with a score of 75 to 24.

Tianjin Wins 800-Meter Relay Race

| Time: One minute, 48 and 5/2 seconds |

Zhou Zhaoyuan Overtakes Guangdong in the End

Liu Changchun and Zhong Lianji Compete Again

First: Tianjin Second: Guangdong

Third: Liaoning Fourth: Shanghai

Yesterday's final of the men's all-around 800-meter relay race included teams from Tianjin, Guangdong, Liaoning, Shanghai, Hubei, Dongte, Zhejiang, and others. The greatest hopes were placed on Liaoning, Shanghai, Tianjin, and Guangdong. As a result, Tianjin won first place, Guangdong second, Liaoning third, and Shanghai fourth, which was beyond most people's expectations. The details of yesterday's final are recorded below:

Four Teams' Lineups

The lineups of the four winning teams yesterday were as follows: Tianjin Team: 1st runner Zhou Ende, 2nd runner Fan Shikui, 3rd runner Wang Yuxiang, 4th runner Zhou Zhaoyuan. Guangdong Team: 1st runner Mai Guozhen, 2nd runner Liu Cheng, 3rd runner Liu Yunqiao, 4th runner Liang Jingping. Liaoning Team: 1st runner Wang Xuanji, 2nd runner Cai Maopu, 3rd runner Teng Ruilin, 4th runner Liu Changchun. Shanghai Team: 1st runner Hao Chunde, 2nd runner Wang Jihuai, 3rd runner Dong Jiaxie, 4th runner Zhong Lianji.

Guangdong Takes the Lead

At the sound of the starting gun, the athletes from each team sprinted forward with all their might. At the start, Tianjin's Zhou Ende was the fastest, Shanghai's Hao Chunde was second, and Guangdong's Li Guozhen was third. At 140-150 meters, Guangdong's Mai Guozhen overtook Shanghai and Tianjin, taking the lead. At the finish line, Guangdong was first, Tianjin second, and Shanghai third, with very little distance between them. Liaoning was in sixth place.

Final Struggle

After the second and third runners took over, the positions of each team did not change much, with Guangdong first, Tianjin second, Shanghai third, and Liaoning sixth. When the last runner took over, it was the highlight of the final. The athletes from each team, such as Liu Changchun, Zhong Lianji, and Zhou Zhaoyuan, were all sprinters, so the struggle was particularly intense. Tianjin's Zhou Zhaoyuan overtook Guangdong's Liang Jingping in the last hundred meters. At the same time, Liu Changchun also tried hard to catch up. At about 112 meters from the finish line, he was less than one meter behind Shanghai's Zhong Lianji. After crossing the finish line, Liu gritted his teeth and barely surpassed Zhong Lianji by one meter, taking third place. Tianjin was first, Guangdong second, and Shanghai fourth, with a time of one minute, 48 and 5/2 seconds.

Chairman Hosts Banquet for Referees

Contributions on the Spot

The chairman and vice-chairman of the National Games hosted a banquet for all the referees at 7 PM last night. Halfway through the banquet, Chairman Dai said that the Games were proceeding smoothly thanks to everyone's support. The work of the sports referees is difficult, and they have been working hard day and night for the past six days. We are very grateful. I feel that sports occupy an important position in education. This Games is sponsored by the central government, and the scale is Fifth Place in Shanghai's Wang Jihuai Photo by Wang Kai

Large and the participation is enthusiastic, which is unprecedented. All the difficult problems that have arisen in the past few days are seen as a daunting task by the staff and referees. If held every year in the future, the experience gained can be used to improve. This is an unavoidable stage in today's infancy of Chinese sports. This is my first contribution to you. Secondly, I hope that experts in sports will change the terminology to Chinese language. You can organize a group to specialize in reviewing various terms and then use the reviewed terminology as the standard language in sports, so that the general public can easily understand it. This is my second contribution to you. Finally, I wish you good health, progress in sports, and a strong nation. The banquet ended at 10 PM.

Delegation Meeting

Several Proposals Passed

On April 5, representatives from various provinces and cities held a meeting and elected Zhang Jiwu as temporary chairman and Ma Zanyi as secretary. The items discussed were: 1. Li Yiusheng from Dongte proposed that a general representative assembly of provinces and cities be organized first, which was passed. 2. Discussed Zhao Wenzao Throwing the Discus, Photo by Wang Kai

The regulations were passed. 3. The Presidium was elected, with Li Yiusheng, Jin Zhaojun, and Ma Zanyi elected to form the Presidium. If anyone leaves Hangzhou, representatives from Shandong and Tianjin, etc. will fill the vacancies. Li Tiejian and Zhong Jun were appointed as secretaries, and Chen Boqing as administrative officer. 4. Jin Zhaojun from Nanjing proposed that the delegation ask the Games to clearly explain the amateur and non-amateur standards and on what regulations they are based and that a reply should be given quickly, which was passed. 5. Zhong Jun from Qingdao proposed that the delegation propose to the Games that the finish line referees should be responsible for the error in the number of laps for athlete number 124 in the 10,000-meter race, which was passed. 6. Dongte proposed Women's Relay Race Hand-Off Photo by Lin Zeren

That the referee's arbitrary decision in the women's relay race should be protested. 7. Li Jiantie, the representative from Hebei, proposed that the Games should announce the types and quantities of prizes received from various regions and the method of distributing the prizes. 8. Beiping proposed the case of No. 504 in the 10,000-meter final. 9. Although General Secretary Ma was responsible for answering the proposal of Guan Sanhao, many have not yet been fulfilled and a clear answer should be requested, which was passed.

The above proposals for the fourth, fifth, sixth, and eighth items, as well as the protest letters from the representatives, were submitted to the Games by the Presidium yesterday. The protests from the representatives are listed below:

Dongte's Proposal The Dongte proposal is to protest the arbitrary refereeing of the finish line referee in the women's 200-meter relay race. The reasons are: (1) The examiner checked the second place referee's form and filled in No. 77 in the grid, then No. 77 is the second place, without any objection. (2) The examiner checked the athlete number column on the first place referee's form and wrote No. 462 in capital letters in the main grid, with a small note above saying "No. 77", which is obviously a later addition. (3) Assuming that No. 462 and No. 77 reached the finish line at the same time, then the referee's form for the second place should be left blank or the number of the third place should be recorded directly.

Shanghai Weile Garden Bicycle Performance

The Shanghai Weile Garden Bicycle Group is the only organization in our country that promotes bicycle racing. They are well-trained in Shanghai, but have never been seen by our people. It is said that the staff of the garden are skilled and pay close attention to their daily life, diet, etc., to ensure that everyone's life is in order to maintain their health. This special trip to Hangzhou to perform at the National Games, which is watched by the whole country, will surely refresh the audience and add color to the Games. Sixteen or seventeen technicians will perform at the track and field at 1:00 PM this afternoon. With the technology of the garden, it will definitely be welcomed by the public. If the Chinese people can pay attention to bicycle racing in the future and achieve excellent results, the program is as follows: (1) Preliminary, four times, two people per group, four laps around the field, (2) Semi-finals, (3) 10,000-meter race, (4) Losers' championship, (5) 15-minute race, (6) Finals.

Bits and Pieces

Understanding the Basics

Zhao Dexin, who won the 10,000-meter championship, whose results have set a new national record, told reporters that since arriving in Hangzhou from Liaoning, he did not dare to eat too much every day, but sipped a little thin porridge, because white rice is not something he is used to, and eating it may affect his stomach and be bad for running, so he would rather endure hunger to win this championship. However, on the night of that day, he ate a lot to compensate for the deficit in his stomach.

Acting as Good News

Shanghai Wang Kai Photo Studio has been taking many photos of various achievements at the Games for days. The washing is very fast. The winning athletes have been buying them to commemorate, and some have sent them back first, acting as good news.

Good Intentions

The women's 200-meter relay was scheduled for 1:00 PM yesterday, and Harbin and Guangdong had a rematch. After mediation, both sides agreed. The four young ladies from Harbin actually used sugarcane as a baton in the rest room to practice the handoff, which can be said to be well-intentioned.

Really Embarrassing

The women's basketball game between Guangdong and Nanjing Special Municipality yesterday was very exciting, but Guangdong won in the end. The audience around applauded and cheered. Before the cheers subsided, a Guangdong Western-dressed youth on the highest row of the west stand sat high on it and repeated several cheers, happy and forgetting himself, almost falling down. A woman of marriageable age below the stand said ("Only heard" him cheering alone, aren't you embarrassed?"

A Big Show

The food needed for the Games every day is as follows: 13 dan of rice, more than 26,000 steamed buns, 50 dan of firewood, 200 jin of soy sauce, 1 dan of soybean oil, 50 jin of salt, 400 jin of bamboo shoots, and more than 200 jin of meat. Such a large account is amazing. The large kitchen needs to prepare 500 to 600 tables every day, and there are a total of 144 cooks and 12 steamed bun makers.

Willing to be Inferior

Yesterday the weather suddenly warmed up, and the audience was sweating profusely, and there were clouds of men and women, and after being scorched by the sun, they felt more charming and lovely, with a spring atmosphere. Fragrant sweat was revealed, and they took out their scented handkerchiefs to wipe it, with the idea of ​​who is fortunate enough to be in the downwind.

News

Various Places Send Personnel to Participate in the National Education Conference

The National Education Conference is not far away. At a time when there are military operations in the North and the South, some outsiders believe that the conference may be affected by the military, and it may be difficult for representatives from various provinces to gather completely. In fact, education has nothing to do with military affairs. In the past, during the warlord era, there were wars between the North and the South, but education was still consistent. A few years ago, the National Education Conference was held in Henan, Beijing and other places, in the autumn of the war between the North and the South. Representatives from various provinces still gathered to express the good spirit of educational unity. Even the northern and remote provinces still sent representatives to participate in the National Education Conference. It is heard that the Ministry of Education has received telegrams from northern and remote provinces in recent days to report on the list of participants, with several starting every day. The probes are recorded below: The Director of the Hebei Provincial Department of Education sent Li Zheng to attend first, the Shanxi Education Office sent Guo Chongzhen, the Sui sent Gong Guohua, the chief of the school education section, the Heilongjiang Department of Education personally attended, the Qingdao Social Bureau Director telegraphed to send the School Education Stock Yesterday's 800-meter Relay Race, Photo by Wang Kai

Director Wang Bingheng to attend the meeting, the Director of the Hunan Department of Education and Huang Dujie, the Director of the Xiangtan Education Bureau, attended together, Zheng Hongnian of Jinan University personally attended, and another message, the Ministry of Education also sent Zhou Gan, Xie Shuying, Wang Jinxin, and Wang Linggen, four gentlemen, to be the editorial section staff of the National Education Conference.

Recent News of the National Boy Scout General Inspection

The reason for holding the general inspection is to promote the purpose of Boy Scout training in China, which is to develop children's ability to do things, cultivate habits of self-reliance and mutual assistance, love of country, nation, and humanity, as well as courage and sacrifice. This aims to make their character noble, their knowledge rich, and their physique sound, so that they can earnestly continue the Three Principles of the People revolution, gradually realizing a nation of, by, and for the people, and ultimately achieving universal harmony. This is not military education. The headquarters of the Chinese Boy Scouts is holding this national general inspection and grand camping event in accordance with the above purposes, to assess past achievements and use them as a basis for future comprehensive improvements. The period is from the 16th to the 21st. In addition to the general inspection ceremony and grand camping, the program includes a supplementary swearing-in ceremony for the commander and various competitions, gatherings, recreational performances, etc., to promote children's outdoor life, connect friendships, increase knowledge, and engage in social service, promoting the spirit of the Boy Scouts under the leadership of the Three Principles of the People, and arousing national attention to the Boy Scout cause. There are no military exercises.

Hunan Boy Scouts Go to Beijing: The Training Department of the Hunan Provincial Party Committee, under instruction, is preparing for the Hunan Boy Scouts to go to Beijing to participate in the national general inspection. Hu Guochun is specially appointed to be responsible for guidance, and Peng Yunbin, Bao Dunpu, Jiang Yinan, Hu Jingsheng, Huang Pinle, and Xia Dexin are assigned to assist. A working office of Boy Scout members from various schools is organized to actively prepare for the selection of one squad from Mingde School and five squads each from Yueyun and Dalü Schools within the province, totaling

one hundred people. They will rehearse various actions to participate in the general inspection. Its organization is divided into five sections: document, management, discipline, communication, and recreation, with one director and several staff members for each section, elected by the participants going to Beijing. An office is formed to oversee everything. The required expenses are subsidized by the government with 800 yuan, allocated for each person's round-trip travel and food expenses (three [角] per person per day).

The remaining expenses are to be borne by each group. The uniform is all yellow clothes, yellow hat, green socks, and leather shoes, with a blue flag with white characters, crowned with the character "湘" (Xiang, for Hunan). It is scheduled to depart from Changsha by train to Hubei on April 8, then transfer to Beijing. It is planned to gather at the Provincial Steering Committee at 3 PM on March 28, and after an inspection in Xinkai Shop outside the South Gate, they will continue camping there for three days and two nights, practicing various outdoor activities. The Provincial Training Department has notified the Boy Scouts of various schools to bring a full set of camping gear to the designated location for gathering, inspection, and practice by the due date.

Instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Regarding Elementary School Teachers

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education instructed the Director of the Songjiang County Bureau of Education, saying: A document was submitted requesting modification of the detailed rules for the examination and certification of elementary school teachers, requesting review and compliance. The matter is understood. The measures for unqualified elementary school teacher training classes were originally established to alleviate the shortage of teachers in various counties. If unqualified elementary school teachers are all replaced without being used, counties with a shortage of teachers will inevitably experience difficulties for a time. Therefore, those who pass the training class are allowed to temporarily serve, but they should still be subject to examination and certification at the time of the examination to determine whether their academic ability is sufficient. Those who pass are given a permit, formally recognized as elementary school teachers. Article 9 of the Jiangsu Provincial Detailed Rules for the Examination and Certification of Elementary School Teachers, previously promulgated by this department,

shows the importance attached to elementary school teachers and the consideration given to the shortage of teachers in various counties. However, Xu Zhenya, Sheng Dan, and others do not understand the situation and want to be exempt from examination and certification, the same as graduates of normal school, based on the strength of half a year of training, which is extremely absurd. The request should not be discussed. The director should clearly explain this. This order.

Opposing British and Dutch Interference in Overseas Chinese Education

The Shanghai Special Municipality Student Union held its 17th meeting yesterday. Those in attendance were Wang Xuequan, Fang Weiren, Li Chunsen, Zhang Bingyan, Li Xiuzhang, Xia Weiqing, and Zhang Tianbai. Wang Xuequan chaired, and Zhang Bingyan took minutes. (4) Proposed by Comrade Wang Xuequan: The Preparatory Committee for the Construction of a Bronze Statue of the Premier by All Circles of Shanghai sent a letter stating that the end of the preparation period is near and hoping to proceed quickly so that results can be achieved on schedule. How should this union handle the fundraising? Resolved: Convene a discussion meeting with those in charge of student unions from various schools to discuss fundraising for the construction of a bronze statue of the Premier. The date is the 9th of this month at 4 PM, and the location is this union. (5) Proposed by Comrade Wang Xuequan: This union should send a telegram to the entire country to unanimously oppose British and Dutch interference in overseas Chinese education. Resolved: Passed. (6) Proposed by Comrade Zhang Bingyan: Student unions in various schools have established night schools for the public and should be commended. Resolved: The Training Department is to draft reward regulations and handle the matter accordingly. The meeting adjourned. Tianjin-Shanghai Women's Basketball Competition. Wang Kai Photography.

Jiangsu Middle School Teachers' Union Petitions for Reorganization of Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office

The Jiangsu Middle School Teachers' Union, concerned that the proposed change of the Education Fund Management Office of more than twenty provinces to the Shanghai-Jiangsu Provincial Education Fund Management Office would affect the education funds of Jiangsu Province, recently sent representatives to the Department of Education and the Provincial Government to petition for it. Secretary Huang of the Department of Education met with the representatives. The representatives stated the petition's opinions. Mr. Huang stated that the Department of Education would never undermine education funds and said that he had submitted a request to the Provincial Government to pay attention. Chairman Ye [of the Provincial Government] received them. Mr. Ye said that the independence of education funds is a matter of course. Since he had come to assume political responsibility for Jiangsu Province, he certainly could not ignore this matter and would request and communicate with the relevant central government agencies. In addition, the representatives pointed out that the central government had previously compensated Jiangsu Province's education funds with 1.8 million yuan of land tax due to the recovery of cigarette tax, but it had not actually been implemented, and that the back wages owed to teachers and staff of various schools had not been paid. They asked the Provincial Government and the Department of Education to find a solution.
