Free Talk

Put it Off with a Laugh

— Hai Ke

Woman: I don't want to marry you anymore. Because I've fallen in love with someone else. This engagement ring, please take it back.

Man: Who is this person? Please tell me.

Woman: I won't tell you. Are you going to make things difficult for him?

Man: No, I'm going to sell this ring to him to avoid losses.

A: Do you prefer beer or champagne?

B: It all depends!

A: Depends on what?

B: It all depends on who's paying the bill! If you're paying, then I'll definitely drink champagne!

Man: I just proposed to you, why did you hesitate? But now you've agreed.

Woman: I wanted to see what your attitude would be after you were disappointed.

Man: What if I'm so disappointed that I just leave? What would you do?

Woman: I didn't think you'd be able to leave, because I already locked the door.

Mother: Child, your neck is black again today, go wash it quickly.

Child: Mother, it's not my neck's fault. It's just that I put on a snow-white new collar, so it looks black in comparison.

Delicacies of Hubei

— Chi Fo

Wuchang Carp Sashimi

I once read a poem by Dongpo, praising "The Yangtze River encircles the city, knowing the fish are delicious."

In recent times, a famous person also wrote the line, "Wine jugs heavily discuss Wuchang fish."

I am quite fond of fish and have always wanted to taste its flavor but had no way to do so. This spring, I traveled to Hubei Province. Together with several friends, I ascended the Yellow Crane Tower. Gazing at the Yangtze River in the distance, the sky and water were the same color. New willows hid crows, fishing boats sang in the evening, and the gentle breeze was warm. The scenery was pleasant. Therefore, I drank with friends at a wine shop to express my traveling pleasure. During the banquet, white clams and green snails, early chives and new bamboo shoots were laid out. The taste was palatable. Following that, a plate of carp sashimi was served. It was fatty, tender, and delicious, far surpassing chicken and pork. Comparing it to pufferfish and the Chinese perch, it seemed even [better]. Only then did I believe that the praise of the ancients was not false. Thus, I ordered more sashimi and drank more wine. The setting sun was about to darken. I returned home drunk. While drinking, I asked the waiter at the wine shop. According to him, the Yangtze River is vast and the water is lively. The fish all taste delicious, but carp is considered the best. Moreover, it must be caught by fishermen below the Yellow Crane Tower, and the eyes must be vermilion in color to be considered authentic. This is because the waters of the Xiang and Han Rivers rush down rapidly and violently until they reach the Yellow Crane Shoal, where they gradually become calm. The fish can rest, and the taste is particularly delicious. If caught elsewhere, even if it is fatty, it is not tender, and even if it is tender, it is not fatty, and it cannot be both.

Hangaog 紫苋 (Purple Amaranth)

East of Hangao's first city's main street, there used to be "Xiao Xiang Lake," also named "Yellow Flower Land." Recently, due to the construction of high dikes upstream in Hubei, the vast sea has become mulberry fields, and the marshland has suddenly become magnificent buildings. Although the marketplaces are prosperous, the fields are still vast. Farmers and gardeners make their living by planting spring chives, autumn cabbage, purple water chestnuts, and silver lotus roots. The soil is fertile and the vegetable gardens are lush. There is a purple amaranth, whose juice is like rouge, beautifully red, and tastes like spring bamboo shoots, but even more crisp and tender. It is a specialty of that area. However, those who carry it on their shoulders and sell it in the streets are all from other places and are all counterfeits. Therefore, buyers must go to the place of origin and pick it from the vegetable beds of the gardeners to get the best product. When the sun is about to set, they tie the grass, store it in baskets, and carry it home in an endless stream. In Hangan customs, on the day of the Beginning of Summer festival, every household prepares dishes with this vegetable to celebrate the season, just like the wormwood wine on the Dragon Boat Festival.

A Record of the Spring Purification Ritual at Plum Garden

— Fei Meng Die

On the day of Geng Wu, my old friend Xie Jiezhi suddenly came from the sea. It had been a year since our parting in Liangxi. I was very happy to see him. He brought a painting of plum blossoms by the owner of Plum Garden as a gift. His elder brother, Gongzhan, painted the branches, and his wife, Shimin, painted the flowers. The inscription was Jiezhi's own calligraphy of his old work, "Ode to Plum Blossoms in the Five Lakes." It was a rare combination of beauty and could be called a "three-perfection." Old friends Bai Xi, Tiao Fu, also came. We spent a long time admiring the painting together. I thought of the wonderful events of admiring plum blossoms under the moon with my friends Shou Juan and others last spring, as if it were happening before my eyes. Now, the plum blossoms have all fallen, and they have become a beloved memory. Fortunately, the peach blossoms are blooming, and the green leaves have not yet provided shade. Moreover, I am glad that I, a former Liu Lang, did not come too late like Du Mu. The host, De Gong, because of the arrival of distinguished guests from afar and because it was the auspicious time for the ancient spring purification ritual, happily invited Jiezhi and myself to tour the garden. We went by car and arrived in an instant. The road through the garden was full of peach blossoms. Yesterday's Sea of Fragrant Snow had suddenly changed into the Red City Glow. Below the Heavenly Heart Terrace, by the edge of the winding pool, several graceful trees were exceptionally enchanting. Vaguely, it was like Xishi of Ruoye, washing silk by the stream, reflecting the shadows of fish. Behind it, there was a white peach tree, whose flowers were particularly abundant. Its crystalline appearance and jade-like purity were captivating. Lady Xi stood silently, and that alone was enough to be enchanting. Jiezhi could not help but recite my poem, "The Kingdom of Guo can only boast of its plain face, how could Wenjun bear to wear red silk." There was also a type of "spotted peach", where each flower had alternating red and white colours, like the powdered faces and rouge marks of a beautiful woman with painted lips - a truly wondrous sight. In front of Song Bin Hall, we met Zhou Jun Jiwei. This gentleman was also an old acquaintance, humorous and interesting, which greatly added to the pleasure of the trip. We drank tea and took a short rest, then went to the study of Zhu Menghua. The room was full of books, and we looked through countless paintings and rubbings by famous artists. The most precious item was the calligraphy of Erquan Shanren brought by Zhou Jilao. To see flowers and this was a great treat for the guests. There was an ancient Qin in the room. Menghua pointed to it and said that it was a gift from a tea boy at the Taihu Hotel. The guests were surprised that such a person could be so refined. I laughed and said, "This is what they call a Nanjing vegetable seller who has the air of the Six Dynasties." As the sun set, we opened a bottle of wine at the Taihu Hotel. The number of guests and the host matched the number of the Seven Sages of the Bamboo Grove. Jilao had experienced military service and spoke at length about the hardships of war and the history of the failure of the warlords during the banquet. His words were passionate and sad, full of colour and sound. The four listeners listened as if they were reading the Book of Han, making it a wonderful accompaniment to the wine. As the feast came to an end, the stars filled the sky, and shadows stretched across the ground. Our trip today was not just like the ancient event at the Orchid Pavilion, but also like Li Bai's spring night banquet in the peach and plum garden. How could this not be recorded?

A Visit to Wang Gang's Personal Pattern Exhibition

— Yu Jianhua

There are many exhibitions held in Shanghai. But never before one dedicated solely to patterns. If so, then Mr Wang Gang's personal pattern exhibition is indeed the first. Although the importance of pattern is known to the Chinese, many neglect it and do not pay attention to it. They watch industry fail and commerce decline, not knowing how to solve the problem from the root. They only sigh at the influx of foreign goods, forgetting that domestic goods are crude and lack artistic thought, unable to arouse the interest of buyers. Therefore, the call to promote domestic goods, although very noisy, is ultimately useless. Mr. Wang Gang once studied

patterns at the Beijing Art School and was already different from others. Later, he went to Tokyo to specialize in pattern design. Not seen for six or seven years, he suddenly opened a personal pattern exhibition at the Ningbo Association. This opened a new era for exhibitions in Shanghai. In the future, as this path develops, this exhibition will be its origin. How can it not be recorded? Moreover, I have also studied this field. The "Method of Pattern," which I wrote, has long been published. So, hearing about this exhibition, I felt like I was hearing a "footstep in an empty valley." The exhibition contains various patterns, about one hundred and fifty pieces. The composition is exquisite, the colors are gorgeous, the ideas are unique, and the tones are harmonious.

It can evoke a warm and pleasant feeling in the viewer. Moreover, it can combine the strengths of the Chinese, Western, and Japanese schools into one, which is even more commendable. There are fewer than ten people in the country who study pattern design, and most of them have a long relationship with me. Mr. Wang is truly a rising star and can be said to have surpassed his predecessors. So, I am happy to introduce him to the people of the country. The exhibition will run until July. Those who are interested in this field, as well as industrialists and merchants, should not miss the opportunity to visit and broaden their horizons. (No remuneration received)

A Record of Viewing Cherry Blossoms and Hearing Cranes

— Zheng Yimei

I wake up very early in the morning, and it is my habit to take a walk of two or three li in the countryside. Nearby is the 63 Garden, which is where I especially like to rest. This is because the burning dust of the city needs to be expelled. There are dozens of cherry trees in the garden, all several fathoms high. Their branches stand tall among the stones, and the scenery is so clear and beautiful it could be painted. These days, the cherry trees are flowering. The flowers have five petals like plum blossoms and are light pink. Those still in bud are even more vibrant, like young women of eighteen or twenty with a hint of spring love. Looking at them makes one's soul melt away. The flowers are either sparse or dense. Looking at them from a distance, they are like mist and clouds. Wandering beneath them, sometimes the wind carries the petals and they land on my clothes, which is even more wonderful. To the left of the bridge, there are two white cranes in the stream, preening their wings. Occasionally they cry, their voices long and drawn out. This is what the ancients meant by the saying, "Cranes cry to the heavens." Many Japanese people live in the garden. One of them, Mr. Matsuoka Sanjiro, speaks fluent Chinese and is quite

friendly with me. He said that the late Wu Changshuo once visited this place and was so fond of the cranes that he immediately painted them. Their red crowns and white feathers, the way they seemed to fly and dance in the clouds, and their carefree and distant spirit were vividly expressed on paper. The painting is still in his suitcase, but Lao Gang has already passed away. Playing with it, I can't help but feel sad.

Red Rug

Miscellaneous Records of Wan Hua's American Tour at the Jade Tassel Chamber

— Lai

Since Wan Hua began performing "Farewell My Concubine" here, playwrights, actors, writers, singers, musicians, theater managers, etc., have come to watch every day without getting tired of it. After the play, they personally go backstage to express their opinions and feelings. One writer said that Mr. Mei's plays have rules and accurate places in every move and action, which are several times higher than American dramas. People say that Chinese dramas are old-fashioned, but from an artistic point of view, they are actually newer than the new American dramas. In the future, American dramas will be greatly affected, or their style will be changed, without a doubt. The president of the Theater Association also said that there are still many actors, singers, and musicians from various theaters here who are eager to see Mr. Mei's plays, but they are suffering from lack of time because they are all performing at the same time. Therefore, they hope that Mr. Mei will add a matinee performance on Thursdays so that all the colleagues in the theater industry can satisfy their desire to see and hear. Although Mr. Mei has matinee performances on Wednesdays and Saturdays, they also have matinee performances, so they still don't have time to spare. (This matter must be agreed to) Some say that "Fen He Wan" is the best because everyone can understand it. Some say that the sword dance posture is the best. Some say that "Ci La La Hu" is the best play. Some say that Chinese drama is very similar to Greek drama. Some say that the rules of Chinese drama are extremely wonderful. For example, at the appropriate time, the audience thinks that they should sing at this time, and the actors on the stage are already singing. There is nothing more pleasing than this. The opinions were numerous and cannot be fully described. Although there are some excessive praises, there are indeed many insightful words.

At the beginning of the performance, several large stores came to ask to display Wanhua's stage costumes in their stores as decorations. They are now displayed in several places, and the number of visitors is unusually crowded. Recently, several large theaters have sent invitations to visit, and the hospitality is extremely warm. Yesterday, a filmmaker came to the theater to shoot newsreels, only shooting a section of "Ci La La Hu." It is said that it will be screened tomorrow night. The entire crew will go to see it, and it is heard that the new film will be available nationwide within three days. Yesterday, we rehearsed "Chunxiang's Trouble at School" to prepare for future changes in the repertoire. "Drunkenness" and "Mulan Joins the Army" must also be performed. "The Legend of Taizhen" may also be re-edited and rehearsed.

Common Sense Gleanings

— Tang Binhua

Do not install a gourd-style light switch with electrical wires on an iron bed. Beware of the electrical wires breaking and coming into contact with the iron bed. It is very easy to cause electrocution to the person sleeping on the bed. How dangerous! This is common sense learned from experience. Do not hang a thermometer in a place where it is exposed to sunlight, because uneven heating will cause the reading to be inaccurate. When a child has hiccups that do not stop, try to make them cry. Then the hiccups will stop. When carrying silver money and encountering a bad person stalking you, just ask a street patrol for the name of a street. Then the bad person will think that you are going to report it to the patrol and will retreat.

Warmth in the Heart (165)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: Red Flames Rise, Prostitutes Admire the Filial Daughter. Red Rug Spread, Instant Meeting with Famous Actors

It was Lu Junfu who helped this group of people. They were unwilling to perform on that kind of shoddy stage. At that time, the new dramas in Shanghai had several problems. First, they didn't read scripts. Second, they didn't divide scenes. It was never clear how many scenes there were. Inside the scene, they were setting up the scenery. Outside the scene, they were still acting. The lights were also not carefully considered. In the boxes and front halls, peddlers selling sweets and fruits were walking back and forth, often obscuring the audience's view. Because many people wouldn't keep their mouths idle while watching the play, they always had to chew on sweet or salty things. Especially in the theater, the noise was a cacophony. It wasn't just the coughing of old men, but also the crying of children. The most annoying thing about that kind of new drama was that it was called "civilized drama." No one knows who decided on the word "civilized." And that group of actors also thought that they were reforming society and that it was a high-class profession. This so-called civilized drama and barbarian drama, no one could define it. At that time, they didn't need a large theatre. As long as it could seat four or five hundred people, it would be enough. They didn't care about the number of the audience, but about the decorum of the audience. There should be no clamor or noise. They would naturally sell tickets to recoup some expenses. But they were different from theater groups that were solely in the business. They had a kind of research nature. They were prepared for everyone to contribute a little money. However, that stage had to be new-fashioned. It didn't matter if it was smaller. All the scenery, the curtains, and the opening and closing of the curtains, had to be fully equipped. Later, they actually found a place. It was a foreign firm selling foreign musical instruments and pianos, called the Moutrie Piano Company. Inside the Moutrie Piano Company, there was a small theatre. Originally, their professions were all related to music. Musicians were related to playwrights. Many musicians living in Shanghai would borrow that place to hold concerts and dances. There was also a kind of opera, but not that kind of large-scale performance. The small theatre, with three or four hundred audience members, was also very good. As for the scenery on the stage, they had ordinary ones, but if they wanted something special, they had to make it themselves. They could also introduce you to scenery-making workers. Fortunately, borrowing his place to perform for a few days was also relatively cheap. Lu Junfu took me to that place and was very proud. Then he signed a contract with them. If the scenery was not enough, he would make one scene himself. Because the drama "Bu Rugui" only had five acts. One or two of them had the same scenery. The rest of the added scenery was also limited. Their performance was only focused on performance. Not focused on the scenery. When the preparations were completed, they selected the date and started the performance. Because Lu Junfu knew Zuo Shichen, he often came to his newspaper office to chat. It was as if he was treating him as an advisor. Discussing new school dramas was especially a pleasure for Lu Junfu.

Yesterday's Shanghai foreign currency interbank call loan rate was 7.2025%, both in the morning and afternoon sessions. and 120,000 in new currency. The Guangdong community continued to load 250,000 in new currency. Hankou loaded 300,000 in hard currency. Recent News on Long-Term Transactions

The six sets of long-term, fixed-term loans issued or deposited around September of the lunar calendar last year, although the country has now adopted the Gregorian calendar, the date of the end of September at that time happened to coincide with the end of October in the Gregorian calendar. Therefore, the fixed term of these term loans differs by exactly one month between the Gregorian calendar and the lunar calendar. They should be fulfilled and delivered around April of this year. However, issuance, deposit, or renewal can still be handled as usual with the agreement of both parties. As such, upon investigation, the long-term loans with fixed terms deposited or issued on September 10th of last year should expire on the 10th of this month. The number of deposits has been verified to reach over 2 million, and the number of loans is no less than 3-4 million. However, because qianzhuang were affected by the Yu Da Zhuang stalemate last month, general depositors have become more cautious and selective. Therefore, there may be a large turnover in the current long-term settlement. For example, if a depositor used to deposit in Qianzhuang A, they may have to move it to Qianzhuang B. As for the loans issued by the qianzhuang at the end of last September, this time, due to market conditions, some who are short on silver must recover all of them for adjustment. If so, then of the long-term deposits expiring on the 10th, it is anticipated that there will be many settlements, and the number of rollovers will be no more than one-third. There is currently no certainty about the interest rate bids. Currently, the banks appear superficially loose, with the silver call loan rate being only a few points, so the deposit interest rate should naturally be inferior to the previous period. If the loan interest rate is owed, it is not surprising that it is slightly higher at five qian per tael due to the small number of issuers or for profit.

Yarn Prices Last Week Were Driven Up by Foreign Yarn

The yarn market was quite weak at the beginning of the week, and the downward trend became more acute, because the bulls in March had no intention of taking delivery, so the sellers put more and more pressure. And thousands of bales of spot goods are in the hands of the shorts, so the market atmosphere at the beginning of the week was bad. The situation became tense again, and retail investors showed panic. Salesmen saw that the overall situation was not good, and they all stood still. Therefore, the lowest price for standard futures yarn this month was 147 taels and 8 qian, and for May, it was 148 taels and 3 qian. At that time, the market had to look at 45 taels. Unexpectedly, American cotton rose, and Toyo Sanpin yarn also rose, and the buyer's mood was slightly boosted. A certain manufacturer's buyer, on Tuesday this month, limited the price to 149 taels, and bought in large quantities, buying 2,300 bales in one day. At the same time, Yunnan merchants developed and bought more than 3,000 bales of 10-count yarn. People's hearts were agitated by it, and the market stabilized. On Wednesday and Thursday, a large household bought 5,600 bales in the near month, so the situation became even tougher. Recently, it has been seen at 151 taels and 8 qian. The yarn market was propped up by the buyers during the Spring Festival holidays on Friday and Saturday, and it will not fall sharply for the time being. However, the situation is urgent and unpredictable, and the future is difficult to consolidate. As a result, the price of each month of standard yarn rose by 2 taels compared with last week. The total transaction volume for the whole week was 69,650 bales. Among the customers, the Yunnan, Niuzhuang, and Guangdong merchants bought the most. Last Week's Cotton Market Was Boosted by Foreign Cotton

The cotton market initially had a flat situation due to sluggish sales, but the shortage of sources from various routes and the tough attitude of the Han merchants have made the market unusually firm. Later, as American and Indian cotton suddenly rose, the combined price was high, and the local shorts could not feel at ease. Activities were launched to buy back short positions, and the market atmosphere suddenly rose. A large household bought more than 10,000 dan of standard cotton to cover short positions in two days. As a result, the price of standard cotton rose by six or seven qian per month compared with the week. The total transaction volume for the whole week was 128,200 dan. The sources on the wharf were 3,820 bales of Tongzhou cotton and 1,260 bales of Yao cotton. Manufacturers bought 14,136 dan of forward and spot goods, and trading firms bought 3,580 dan. However, yesterday's market was determined by the seller's skills, because there were also those that did not fall. Observing the market situation, japonica rice is quite stagnant and weak, and the road for thin rice is very sluggish, so the market is depressed and gradually eroded. High-quality goods are only around 18 yuan and 7 jiao. There is a shortage of both river goods and old indica rice, and since the incoming goods are not prosperous, the producing market is still stable. Therefore, although the sales in this port are extremely numb, the price is still stable. Only the goods with secondary color have been slightly reduced. The kebu indica rice is completely crushed by foreign rice, so the zero discount is not very refreshing. Large dishes stand firm due to the rarity of arrivals, and the change of the yuan is negative. Both sales are even, and both are fresh and disgraceful.

Hunan: River downstream boats have been slightly connected since the weather cleared up. The import intention of each party varies. There is a discretion in the movement of japonica rice in Changxi Machine, but after the weakness of the north market, the price is extremely tight, so the market has unknowingly lost its spectrum.

There are few arrivals of white japonica rice from Suzhou and Tong. There are few tastes in rural villages, and the market price of high-quality goods is slightly repaired. The middle and secondary are soft. The sales of thin rice and early rice from the four townships of the South Merchants are sluggish, and the selection is strict and picky. The situation is therefore depressed, and the high and secondary are all downstream. The sheep indica rice is scarce in this area, and buyers are watching. The market price is flat. Duzi indica rice and passenger plane tips sell more actively. The store tastes are still active, and the market is still stable. The circulation of the general change is active. There are few arrivals, so the sellers sell them, and the price is tight. Check that there is not much change in the north and south markets in these two days. In addition, the Rice and Grain Price Evaluation Committee has recently been established, and the rice market will probably not be easy to rise in the future.

Due to the gold price relationship and the sufficient economic power of Japanese silk merchants, they are expanding the amount of silk in stock, and the degree of silk price decline is limited. At the beginning of the week, the transfer of Chinese silk was not weak. However, due to the unpredictable fluctuations in foreign exchange, European merchants did not dare to take risks and buy more. The bottom of dry cocoons was getting thinner day by day, and the price of cocoons was tending to be firm. The remaining goods of Chinese merchants were insufficient, and the source of Sichuan and Shandong provinces was not continued. The International Anti-Narcotics Conference Passed a Resolution on International Cooperation in Anti-Narcotics

Proposed by Mr. Wu Kaisheng, Representative of China

The 13th session of the International Anti-Narcotics Committee was held from January 20 to February 14 of this year in the Secretariat of the Japanese League of Nations in Geneva. Mr. Wu Kaisheng, the Chinese representative, delivered a speech at the meeting, expressing the determination of the Chinese National Government to strictly prohibit opium and other narcotic drugs, and the implementation of the ban throughout the country, which was deeply supported by the committee. Wu argued that the governments of all countries should sincerely cooperate with the Chinese government to jointly seek a ban. Fortunately, this was passed by the committee. The original draft submitted by Wu and the original text passed by the committee are recorded as follows: (1) Original draft submitted by our country: The Anti-Narcotics Advisory Committee is aware that China has suffered greatly from the smuggling of narcotic drugs, which is prohibited by the Hague Convention of 1912. Moreover, the Chinese government feels it is difficult to prohibit smuggling under the current situation. According to the provisions of Chapter 4 of the Hague Convention of 1912, the Chinese government and the governments of all countries that have treaty relations with China should take concerted action to prohibit the scourge of opium and narcotic drugs. Due to the development of smuggling in China and its recent phenomena, it is believed that close cooperation in this regard is particularly necessary at this time. Therefore, the Executive Yuan is requested to remind the governments of the countries concerned of the provisions of the aforementioned Hague Convention and to request the governments of each country to take appropriate measures to effectively implement the provisions. It was also decided to include the situation of narcotic drugs in China on the agenda of the next meeting. (2) Resolution passed by the Anti-Narcotics Committee of the League of Nations on February 11, 1919: The Anti-Narcotics Advisory Committee is aware that China has suffered greatly from the smuggling of narcotic drugs, which is prohibited by the Hague Convention of 1912. Moreover, the Chinese government feels it is difficult to prohibit smuggling under the current situation. According to the provisions of Chapter 4 of the Hague Convention of 1912, the Chinese government and the governments of all countries that have treaty relations with China should take concerted action to prohibit the scourge of opium and narcotic drugs. Due to the development of smuggling in China and its recent phenomena, it is believed that close cooperation in this regard is particularly necessary at this time. Therefore, the Executive Yuan is requested to inform the countries that have treaties with China of this matter, and it is recommended that the Chinese government and the countries that have treaties with China jointly study the current situation of narcotic drugs smuggled, and the countries that have treaties with China should find ways to implement the provisions of Chapter 4 of the Hague Convention, and the next Advisory Committee should consider this issue. It was also decided to include the situation of narcotic drugs in China on the agenda of the next meeting.

Overseas Chinese Merchants in Vietnam Telegraphically Request Prompt Resolution of French Onerous Taxes

So That Hua Silk Can Be Shipped to the Market

The silk industry in this port, because the French government in Vietnam violated the treaty and increased the tax on Hua silk entering the country from 7% to 50%, resulting in the inability to transport and sell it. Although it had sent representatives to Beijing to petition and telegraphed repeatedly to request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to make serious representations to the French Minister to China, it has not been resolved for a year. The industry received a telegram from overseas Chinese merchants in Vietnam, such as Nianji, roughly stating that the spring season is now approaching, and there is a great need for domestic silk here. The existing stock has been exhausted. Japanese goods are light in material and cannot last long. It is hoped that the government will immediately negotiate with the French Minister and resolve the issue promptly so that the goods can be transported to Vietnam for sale. Otherwise, the silk industry, which has a long history, will be wiped out from now on, etc. After receiving the telegram, the industry heard that it intends to send representatives to Beijing again to make a final appeal and petition, so that it can be resolved immediately to facilitate commercial transportation.

Meeting on How the Silk Industry Deals With Foreign Firms

Reforming Various Old Habits

Electing Representatives for Negotiation

The Shanghai Silk Cocoon Association and the Shanghai Silk Factory Association Organizing Committee, because according to reports from the industry, after the implementation of public measurement procedures for silk unloading by various foreign firms, various difficulties and nitpicking have occurred, specifically convened a temporary emergency meeting of all silk factory peers in Shanghai at 3:00 pm yesterday. More than 80 people attended. Huang Jinchen and Shen Huachen served as chairmen. After performing the rituals, the chairman first announced the purpose of the meeting, roughly stating that since the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau implemented the public measurement inspection of factory silk for export, various foreign firms, adhering to their habits and adopting sampling silk, still extracted one strip from each piece as before, and did not give receipts for shaking strips, and after the silk was loaded in canvas bags, the silk building still demanded oil paper white slips, etc., and did not fulfill the Shanghai business negotiation method. Now that various peers have sent letters requesting negotiation, it should be discussed. After mutual discussion by the peers, it was generally agreed that the silk buildings of various foreign firms did not follow the business negotiation methods to handle matters, and various elements were temporarily generated, which was really hateful. It was decided that only two strips should be allowed to be sampled for every five pieces of sample silk. Starting from April 1, the excess sample silk taken by each foreign firm should be returned in full. For the extracted shaking strips, the foreign firm should make a receipt for the people, indicating the number of strips and the weight, and still weigh and count when returning them. For silk loaded on Saturday, the silk payment will be paid on the morning of this day. After using canvas bags, the oil paper white slips that have always been used will be abolished immediately and will no longer be supplied. Chairman Shen said that the above decisions will be negotiated with the Export Silk Association based on reason, and it will be urged to earnestly fulfill them. At present, please be patient. From now on, do not be able to accommodate any unexpected demands from the silk building, so as not to make excuses. Next, it was discussed that Bao Tai Silk Factory and 12 other factories requested the Inspection Bureau to forward a letter, and the number of pounds and ounces on the public quantity list should be distributed and noted, and all foreign firms should be notified to eliminate the habit of rounding off, and to refer to the Japanese precedent of using four taels as a unit (ie, two out of ten and five), and not to arbitrarily deduct it, so as to initiate disputes and maintain interests. The case was passed. Finally, Chairman Shen reported that the public measurement inspection is related to laws and regulations, and the industry should jointly abide by it. If the buyer and seller have private contacts and settle the price by net weight, the inspection authorities have considerable punishment. All our peers should pay attention and not make mistakes. The meeting was adjourned and it was already half past five.

Why We Must Punish the Rebel Yan Xishan

At this time of recent unification and before the people's suffering has subsided, how should all our comrades and compatriots throughout the nation unite as one to support the Central Government, consolidate the unification, enable the implementation of disbandment and reorganization, the progress of political tutelage, and the realization of construction? In the past year, disasters and turmoil have repeatedly arisen. The rebellious elements of Gui, Zhang, Feng, and Tang successively raised armies and betrayed the Party and the country, causing repeated disruptions to peaceful unification. Fortunately, relying on the loyalty and bravery of our Party's soldiers and all comrades, united as one, and the sincere support and assistance of the compatriots throughout the nation, we were finally able to quickly suppress the rebellious bandits who betrayed the Central Government, endangered the Party and the country, isolated themselves from the Party and the country, and isolated themselves from the masses. We were celebrating the thorough elimination of reactionary forces within the country, the permanent preservation of peaceful unification, and the opportunity for compatriots throughout the nation to live and work in peace, rest and recuperate. Unexpectedly, the rebel Yan Xishan, at a time when the border defense was strained and the remaining rebels had not yet been completely eliminated, again arbitrarily put forward propositions, coerced the Central Government, gathered the remnants of warlords, communist bandits, and all reactionary elements in Taiyuan, indiscriminately issued circular telegrams, instigated chaos to harm the country, moved troops, arrested party members, and closed down the Party and government organs of the Central Government in Peiping and Tientsin. The Central Government, with magnanimity, repeatedly tolerated this, and even though his rebellious intentions were already evident, it did not hastily issue an order for his punishment, hoping that he could still awaken and repent, to avoid further war and preserve the vitality of the country. However, the beastly nature of the rebel Yan could never be changed, and his warlord ambition could never be restrained. Recently, he has intensified his efforts, acting perversely, outwardly claiming to go abroad, but secretly preparing for war, letting Feng return to Shaanxi, and actually mobilizing troops. This is the action of someone who has lost his mind and is plotting rebellion, willing to bear the crime of undermining peaceful unification, and willing to be a successor to Gui, Feng, Zhang, and Tang. In order to maintain the discipline of the Party and the country and consolidate unification and peace, the Central Government has truly reached the point of being unable to tolerate it any longer and unable to forgive it any longer. It has no choice but to issue a clear order for his punishment and to eliminate the treacherous and villainous elements. During this period of suppressing the rebellion, we must deeply understand and actively promote the crimes of the rebel Yan in betraying the Party and harming the country, as well as the significance of the punishment. I will now enumerate them on the left as a declaration to the people of the country.

(1) The Crimes of Yan Xishan in Betraying the Party and Harming the Country

1. Seizing Power and Position in the Name of Revolution: Before the Xinhai Revolution, when Yan Xishan was studying in Japan, he once joined the Tongmenghui, but after returning to China, he served as the standard commander of the First Standard of the Shanxi New Army, willingly serving as a servant of the Manchu Qing Dynasty, and no longer had the revolutionary cause in his heart. On September 8th of the Xinhai Revolution, the Jin Army launched an uprising. Yao Yijia, the battalion commander of the Second Standard of the New Army, led all the officers and soldiers to break through the provincial capital, and then used one company to attack the Manchu city, one company to attack the governor's yamen, and one company was personally led by Yao, providing support in the middle. After a day of hard fighting, the governor of Shanxi was killed. At the same time, the Manchu city was also captured, but Yao's subordinates also suffered heavy losses, with only a few dozen people remaining. Before that, Huang Guoliang, the standard commander of the Second Standard, had already been ordered to leave the provincial capital. Yan Xishan, possessing all the soldiers of the standard, remained stationed and did not move, with the intention of waiting for an opportunity to harm the revolutionary army and seek credit from the Qing Dynasty. When he heard that the Manchu city had been captured and the governor had been killed, he urgently ordered his subordinates to occupy the gunpowder bureau, armory, and other places, and then declared that he was a member of the Tongmenghui and was willing to cooperate with Yao. He then took the opportunity to send private cronies to carry out activities everywhere, inviting the officers who initiated the uprising to a meeting at the former Provincial Assembly. Because he possessed the power to mobilize troops, he was publicly elected as the temporary commander-in-chief, occupying the territory of Shanxi and becoming its local emperor for more than ten years.

2. Slaughtering Comrades and Encouraging Yuan to Become Emperor: After Yan Xishan seized the territory of Shanxi in the name of the Tongmenghui, he immediately bribed and colluded with the Beiyang warlords. When Yuan Shikai obtained the title of Grand President by deceit, Yan the rebel flattered him in every possible way, and was extremely attentive. In order to consolidate his position, he first declared his withdrawal from the Party and devoted himself to slaughtering revolutionary comrades and disbanding revolutionary organizations. The arrest of comrades Zhang Shixiu and Li Wufeng, and the massacre of revolutionary comrades in the Hedong Incident, almost wiped out the revolutionary forces in the north led by the Premier of our Party. He also often advocated the absurd idea that the military state and the empire were complementary, and that the empire must be rebuilt before a military state could be created, in order to promote Yuan Shikai's autocratic ideas and encourage his ambition to become emperor. When the Preparatory Committee was established, in addition to contributing two million yuan himself, he also persuaded a Shanxi ticket dealer to donate three million yuan. Fearing that the rebel Yuan would not completely trust him, he also sent his parents to Beijing as hostages, and then sent personnel to persuade Yuan to advance, and was the first to become Yuan’s subject. Yuan Shikai then announced the imperial system. The Republic of China, which the revolutionary martyrs had exchanged for with their heads and blood, was almost interrupted because of Yuan's declaration of the imperial system. Tracing back to the culprit, it was all caused by the rebel Yan Xishan's conspiracy and instigation.

3. Exploiting People's Wealth in the Name of Village Governance: Yan the rebel is inherently greedy and cunning, and has employed countless schemes. For more than ten years of governing Shanxi, he has promoted village governance. The people of the country value what they hear and despise what they see, and through misrepresentation, they have given him the reputation of being a model governor. In fact, the village governance he has implemented is purely a paper exercise. According to recent reports from social organizations in various places, his so-called village governance is simply using village chiefs who are over forty or fifty years old and addicted to opium to extort money from the local people. In short, he uses the village chiefs as his personal tools for accumulating and extorting wealth. Two years ago, Yan the rebel sent his nephew with a portion of the wealth he had accumulated over the years, totaling twenty million yuan, to be deposited in a French bank. Later, because his nephew indulged in extravagance in France, he died of excessive indulgence. The French bank then confiscated his deposit (on the grounds that the deposit was in the name of the nephew and not in the name of Yan, and now that the nephew is dead, it should be taken over as public property of France). Yan the rebel was extremely distressed. Last autumn, when Feng the rebel mutinied, the reason why he claimed to accompany Feng abroad was to personally negotiate with France for the return of this large amount of unjustly taken deposit. Now that there is no hope of recovering this matter, he is again plotting evil and engaging in endless extortion. In the past year, Yan the rebel has occupied the territories of the four provinces of Shanxi, Hebei, Chahar, and Suiyuan, and his income has been even greater. He regards Hebei as a colony and orders it to pay two million yuan in cash every month. He still thinks this is not enough and issues banknotes indiscriminately in Shanxi in order to absorb the cash of the four provinces. His greed, cruelty, cunning, and poisonousness are unprecedented.

4. Destroying Education and Practicing Ignorance: The education in Shanxi can be summed up in one sentence: "Education for the policy of keeping the people ignorant." The purpose of its education, ostensibly military-nationalist democracy, is actually to make the people of Shanxi slaves and docile citizens of Yan the rebel. This is exactly the same as Feng Yuxiang's training of soldiers, making them only know Commander-in-Chief Feng. Yan the rebel also established a talent cultivation center in Taiyuan. All students graduating from any school at home and abroad must enter the center for two years. He must tame them and train them to be running dogs before giving them the opportunity to work. Otherwise, he will either drive them out of the country or find ways to make them addicted to opium in order to destroy their ambition and ability. He even induces students in elementary, middle, and high schools to smoke opium, making it a fashion. The purpose of this is not to simply keep the people ignorant, but to destroy the people, so that the people of Shanxi will be deeply poisoned, lose all their vitality, have no revolutionary ideas, and have no revolutionary ability, so that he can maintain his position forever and be the local emperor of Shanxi for a long time.

5. Disrupting Transportation and Disturbing Finance: Since Yan Xishan opportunistically joined our Party in the autumn of the seventeenth year of the Republic, his various crimes are too numerous to record. For the past two years, he has been extracting subsidies and detaining vehicles on the Peiping-Hankow and Peiping-Suiyuan Railways almost every day, causing the finances of the two railways to be on the verge of bankruptcy. According to the current reports, the amount of subsidies taken from the Peiping-Hankow and Peiping-Suiyuan Railways totals more than 5.5 million yuan. The amount taken from the Peiping-Suiyuan and Zhengtai Railways from December of the seventeenth year of the Republic to July and August of last year is also no less than 400,000 yuan, and the unreported amounts are not included. As for the vehicles he has detained along the Peiping-Hankow Railway in recent years, the number has reached hundreds, and they have never been returned to the railway bureau, causing the traffic on the Peiping-Hankow Railway to decline day by day and become unmanageable. In short, Yan the rebel occupies the north, forcibly occupies the Peiping-Hankow and Peiping-Suiyuan Railways, regards them as private property, disregards the country, and flouts the law. He also connives at the military, selling car skins at will and forcing down the price of Shanxi coal transportation to fill his own pockets, causing the business of the Peiping-Hankow and Peiping-Suiyuan Railways to plummet. In the past, the annual revenue of the Peiping-Hankow Railway was at least more than 30 million yuan, but last year the total revenue was only about 10 million yuan. The revenue of the Peiping-Suiyuan Railway was also more than 9 million yuan in the past, but last year it was less than 5 million yuan. Recently, Yan the rebel also detained the through train on the northern section of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway and various passenger trains to transport troops, and monitored telegrams and hijacked railway affairs. The tracks and iron bridges south of Dezhou were also bombed. His crimes of disrupting transportation are even worse than those of Feng and Tang. Since the founding of the Republic of China, warlords have been dividing and occupying territory, and there have been years of war. The only place that has been able to maintain peace and avoid war is Shanxi. According to the usual assumption, the economic situation and the people's livelihood in Shanxi must be better than in other provinces. However, the facts show us exactly the opposite. The Shanxi Provincial Bank is issuing irredeemable banknotes in such large quantities that probably no one except the Shanxi Provincial Finance Authorities knows the exact number. In order to reorganize the banknotes of the Shanxi Provincial Bank, the Central Government previously approved the issuance of 24 million yuan of Shanxi financial public bonds for financial reorganization to provide relief. However, recently Yan the rebel has again adopted the method of concentrating cash and indiscriminately issuing large amounts of banknotes, prohibiting the export of cash, making the financial situation even more chaotic and the people more and more miserable. Fortunately, the Central Government has now decided to cancel this debt, and it has not been put into circulation. Otherwise, the people of Shanxi would have suffered even greater losses.

6. Inciting Feng and Tang to Disrupt Unification: Yan the rebel is inherently fond of chaos. The successive rebellions of Feng Yuxiang and Tang Shengzhi in the past year were all caused by his conspiracy and instigation. Last autumn, on August 14th of the lunar calendar, when Feng was in Jinci, Yan sent a telegram to Feng, saying that tomorrow was the Mid-Autumn Festival, and invited him to enjoy the moon together. The next day, Yan hosted Feng at a banquet in Jinci, where he incited Feng to betray him in every possible way. Feng was initially quite unenthusiastic, but after Yan repeatedly urged him, he was finally moved. They immediately agreed that Feng would be responsible for military affairs and Yan would be responsible for political affairs, and they planned everything. When the troops of Song Zheyuan, Sun Liang, and others under Feng failed to raise troops, and the Central Army forced their way to Tongguan, Yan knew that nothing could be done, so he issued a circular telegram expressing his absolute support for the Central Government and declaring that he would punish Feng, but he did not send a single soldier. Later, when the troops of Shi Yousan mutinied in Pukou, Yan again came up with a strange idea and sent Zhao Pi-lian to persuade Tang Shengzhi to issue a telegram to resist the Central Government. Tang Shengzhi sent a representative, Yuan, to discuss with him, and it was decided that Yan would be responsible for the Party and government, and Tang would command the remnants of the Northwest Army. Yan then sent a telegram to Feng, saying that Tang Shengzhi had now awakened, but wanted your troops to be under his command. Feng agreed, and then recognized and gave Tang 500,000 yuan for mobilization expenses. After consulting back and forth, the matter was delayed, and Tang rebelled against the Central Government with his electrical telegram. However, there were slight discrepancies with what Yan had advocated, and he only received 250,000 yuan for mobilization expenses. Later, when Yan saw the Central Army besieging from all sides and that Tang could not support it, he again sent a telegram supporting the Central Government and turned to declare that he would punish Tang, sitting back and reaping the benefits. In the past year, he has made others clamor and rush forward, while he has issued instructions from behind. If they succeed, he will reap the benefits; if they fail, they will suffer the consequences. His cunning and treachery are truly unparalleled.

7. Arbitrarily Making Propositions and Taking the Opportunity to Instigate Chaos: Yan the rebel's joining of our Party and engaging in the National Revolution has become increasingly opportunistic. His feudal ideas have not changed at all. Recently, he has been plotting reaction and repeatedly making absurd remarks. First, he advocated giving way to the country and being responsible in retirement. Then, he changed from being responsible in retirement to organizing a council of elders and a privy council consisting of the commanders-in-chief of the First, Second, Third, and Fourth Group Armies. Finally, he advocated that the executive and supervisory committee members of the First, Second, and Third National Congresses should be jointly responsible, and that all party members should vote to resolve party issues. To give way to the country is to regard the country as the private property of one or two people, which can be privately transferred at will. This is completely the mindset of a family dynasty. As for being responsible in retirement, it is even more contradictory, because being in retirement and being responsible are absolutely incompatible. Examining the motivation behind his remarks, it is nothing more than using the good name of the Party and the country to coerce Chiang Kai-shek, a comrade who is loyal to the masses and upholds Party rule, to retire and abandon the responsibility of the revolution, and then to reinstate Pu Yi, Duan Qirui, Wu Peifu, Zhang Zongchang, and others who have been selling the country and harming the people for decades to come to power, first destroying our Party and then destroying China. As for advocating that the commanders-in-chief of the First, Second, Third, and Fourth Group Armies and others should organize a council of elders and a privy council to oversee everything, it is directly advocating that military autocracy should replace democratic centralism, and it has already exposed its true colors as a warlord, which is tantamount to a confession of betraying the masses. Combining the executive and supervisory committees of the First, Second, and Third Central Committees in one place not only violates the Party Constitution, but also intends to gather reactionary elements who have been lawfully expelled from the Party by the Central Committee, such as Mao Zedong, Tan Pingshan, Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, Feng Yuxiang, and Chen Gongbo, to the Central Committee, so that the Third International Communist Party reorganization faction and feudal warlords can once again bring disaster to the Party and the country. As for the general vote of party members, what Party Constitution does it follow? What precedents does it cite? It is absurd and ridiculous, and enough to make people laugh. The rebel is making such preposterous remarks, directly unaware of the Party, and even more unaware of the country. His intention is nothing more than to take this opportunity to instigate chaos.

8. Colluding with Reactionaries and Threatening the Party and the Country: In the past month, the road to Taiyuan has been filled with carriages and horses. Guo Chuntao and Wang Faqin, representatives of the reorganization faction, Pan Yizhi, representative of the Gui clique, Bian Shoujing, representative of Qi Xieyuan, Zou Lu, representative of the Western Hills Conference faction, Wu Guangxin, representative of the Anfu clique, and representatives of bandits, and representatives sent by Japanese imperialists, have all gathered in Taiyuan, spreading rumors and creating illusions. Yan the rebel treats these representatives with great respect, housing them in separate residences and treating them as honored guests. They hold joint meetings in the Zisheng Hall every day to discuss methods of betraying the Central Government and endangering the Party and the country, bringing together the great achievements of imperialist warlords, bandits, and all corrupt and greedy elements. If they were to succeed by chance, not only would the current situation of peaceful unification be completely destroyed, but the state of disintegration and separation of the past ten years would be restored, and disasters would invade and engulf the country and the nation in an abyss of no return.

9. Closing Down Party Headquarters and Arresting Party Members: After Yan the rebel issued a telegram, although the party headquarters in Peiping and Tianjin were under feudal forces, they were still able to work hard in the spirit of the Premier's great fearlessness, refuting the non-unification in his telegram, and printing and distributing various publications clarifying that peace cannot be discussed without unification, and construction cannot be discussed without peace, and posting various bulletins and slogans to correct the people's vision. Yan the rebel then secretly ordered the troops in Peiping and Tianjin to close down the party headquarters in the two special municipalities of Peiping and Tianjin and Hebei Province, and forcibly ordered them to stop working, and arrested Lu Dangping, the Minister of Propaganda of the Tianjin Special Municipality Party Department, and Jia Yi, the Reorganization Committee Member of Hebei Province. He also sent troops to occupy the North China Daily, the propaganda organ of the Central Committee in Peiping and Tianjin, and the Central News Agency branch, and arrested its director, Yin Shuxian. This kind of vicious and cruel means of destroying Party affairs and undermining the revolution, which the rebels Feng and Tang had previously been afraid to do, Yan the rebel brazenly did it without regard for the consequences, and his crimes were actually greater than those of Feng and Tang.

10. Publicly Claiming to Go Abroad, but Secretly Planning to Invade Southwards: After Yan Xishan issued absurd remarks, the people of the whole country attacked him. The Central Government, with magnanimity, sought only peace and did not pursue the past. It listened to his voluntary resignation and gave him preferential treatment. However, Yan the rebel harbored evil intentions and did not repent until his death. On the one hand, he declared to the Central Government that he would retire and go abroad, but on the other hand, he was still holding military meetings in Taiyuan, inciting his subordinates to send telegrams to retain him. On the one hand, he encouraged Feng Yuqin to return to Tongguan and send troops to invade the east. At the same time, he was also conscripting new recruits in Hebei, preparing to invade southwards. Yan the rebel believes that this move will preemptively attack, but he does not know that the more obvious the crime of betraying the Party and harming the country is, the faster his elimination and demise will be. This is evidenced by the facts of the past, which are unmistakably true.

11. Colluding with Foreigners, Selling the Country and Seeking Help: Since the founding of the Republic of China, the Beiyang warlords have been fighting and killing each other, repeatedly retaliating for more than ten times. Yan the rebel has been in between, colluding with both sides, and has never made a clear expression. Although this is due to his inherently treacherous nature, his mediocrity and cowardice are also a factor. In the war against Feng in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the people of the country believed that it was against the norm. In fact, Yan the rebel dared to launch the attack purely because he was instigated and secretly assisted by Japanese imperialism. Because Tu Ni was a direct descendant of the pro-Japanese Duan system, Duan was expelled by the Feng faction, so he lobbied Japan to instigate Yan the rebel to oppose Feng. This rebellion is the same. Yan the rebel intends to betray the Central Government and wants to get the help of Japan. Japan wants to actively invade North China, so it uses Yan the rebel as a puppet, and Lu Zongyu and others are in the middle to bring them together, so they conclude a kind of treaty of betrayal. The content of the treaty is that Japan will provide Yan the rebel with as much financial and military equipment as possible to resist the Central Government and establish a government in Peiping, and Yan the rebel will promise to give Japan the mining rights of the most profitable mines in Shanxi and the construction rights of the Inner Mongolia Railway as a reward. This treaty was established two months ago. In addition to successively transporting various military equipment to Shanxi, Japan has also secretly dispatched personnel from the General Staff Headquarters to be stationed in Taiyuan, Tianjin, and Peiping to plan military affairs for Yan the rebel. The strategy of Yan the rebel's three-way southward invasion was adopted according to the suggestions of the Japanese staff. Yan the rebel knew that the southward invasion might not succeed, so he prepared for a long-term plan, and also borrowed 20 million yuan from American, French, and Belgian companies, half in cash and half priced in flour. A part of it has been transported from Tianjin to Shanxi. The 2 million yuan and 300,000 bags of flour that Yan the rebel allocated to Feng the rebel were part of this loan. In short, in order to betray the Central Government and satisfy his ambition, Yan the rebel does not hesitate to sacrifice the people of North China and does not hesitate to sacrifice national sovereignty as the price. His crime of selling the country and seeking help is even worse than Feng the rebel's collusion with Soviet Russia and the loss of Mongolia and Xinjiang.

(2) Our Understanding and Efforts in Punishing Yan Xishan

1. Yan the rebel is essentially a remnant of the Beiyang warlords who is fickle, unprincipled, and shameless. The reason why our Party gave him preferential treatment when he returned two years ago was to give him the opportunity to improve himself and to influence him with the personality of the Premier and the sincerity of comrades, hoping that he would change his ways from now on and be on the right track, and make some contributions to redeem his past sins. However, Yan the rebel's beastly nature cannot be changed after all. Since he joined our Party, he has appeared loyal and honest, but in reality he is unpredictable. In the past two years, he has been a monster and a ghost, and his treachery is unparalleled. He has used the people who are trusted by the Central Committee to engage in sabotage and rebellion, and has destroyed the revolution in the name of revolution, colluding with imperialists and corrupt forces, betraying the Party and the country, destroying peaceful unification, willingly being the leader of the Rong, and being vicious and poisonous. He has not repented until his death. He has isolated himself from the Party and isolated himself from the country. Therefore, we must quickly issue a clear order and carry out a large-scale attack to rectify the discipline of the country and maintain the righteousness of the world.

2. At present, the most urgent demands of the people are national peace and unification, and the necessary conditions for carrying out political tutelage and construction and completing the national revolution are also national peace and unification. Only with peaceful unification can we restore the vitality of society, and only with unification can we establish national power. Peaceful unification is the fundamental policy formulated by the Central Committee based on the actual needs of the people. Those who vigorously implement this policy are friends of the people, and those who violate this policy are enemies of the people. The reason is very clear. The recent outrageous remarks made by Yan the rebel, and his vicious and treacherous actions in the past year, are all aimed at destroying peace and unification. In this era of Party rule, those who violate the discipline of our Party, flout national laws and regulations, and plot to destroy peace and unification are creating chaos. Conversely, those who obey the orders of the Central Committee, abide by national laws, eliminate traitors and bandits who endanger the Party and the country, and maintain national peace and unification are suppressing chaos. The Central Committee, in accordance with the teachings of the Premier, is engaged in revolutionary construction, and it cannot but launch a vigorous punitive expedition against this chaotic feudal warlord, eliminate the fierce and stubborn elements, consolidate the unification of the country, and ensure the victory of the revolution, so that political tutelage can be promoted and construction can be implemented, and to establish a new model of China together with our compatriots throughout the country.

3. Our Party is a revolutionary political party that is trusted and supported by the people of the whole country. As shown by the past facts, those who obey the Central Committee survive, and those who betray the Central Committee perish. Previously, the rebels of the Gui clique and Feng and Tang had territories that were not wide and troops that were not numerous. However, once they betrayed the Central Committee, they were abandoned by the people of the whole country and swept away by the revolutionary armed forces. Within a month, they were completely eliminated. The end of Yan the rebel will be no exception. However, Yan the rebel has been entrenched in Shanxi for a long time and has deep roots. Recently, he has recruited corrupt elements and blusters. Although his strength is not enough to shake the Central Committee and endanger the Party and the country, his rampage and stubborn struggle are enough to prolong the war and increase the suffering of the people of the country. We, the people of the whole country, should recognize that this punishment of Yan the rebel is the fundamental elimination of the remnants of the Beiyang warlords by our Party, and the final decisive battle between the revolution and the counter-revolution. Once this remaining Beiyang warlord Yan is eliminated and the united corrupt forces are crushed at the same time, the roots of reaction will be forever eradicated, the unification of the country will be ensured, construction will be carried out smoothly, and political tutelage will be realized as scheduled. The people of the four provinces of Shanxi, Hebei, Chahar, and Suiyuan have long been under the violence of Yan the rebel and have suffered from the exploitation and destruction of the enemy. In order to eliminate suffering and reduce the war, they should unite as one, launch a joint effort, and assist the Central Committee in eliminating this disaster, the rebellious Party, and the traitorous and harmful bandit.

The Chinese Martial Arts Association Adds Wrestling Class

The Shanghai Chinese Martial Arts Association was founded in the eighth year of the Republic of China and has long been a prestigious national martial arts organization in Shanghai. Since the summer of the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, after revising its constitution and changing to a committee system, Luo Shuqing, the training director, has been teaching various national martial arts diligently and meticulously. He teaches two hours each in the morning and evening, from 6:00 AM to 8:00 AM at the public sports ground outside the West Gate, and from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM at the Puyi Society in Dadongmen. Recently, recognizing the important position of wrestling in national martial arts, a special class will be added starting this month to foster talent. Those interested in national martial arts can register and join at the above two locations.

Two Lost Boys Awaiting Collection

The Municipal Public Security Bureau has sent a lost boy named Qiu Dacheng from the Second Precinct of the Sixth District. According to inquiries, he is eleven years old and from Jiangbei. He does not know his address, street name, house number, or family situation. The boy is wearing a broken floral cotton-padded jacket and striped cotton pants, with no shoes or socks. He has now been transferred to the Women and Children's Relief Association for care and collection.

Also, a lost boy named Li Amao has been sent from the Second Precinct of the Fifth District. According to inquiries, he is nine years old and lives at No. 10, Xin Caofang, Yongxing Road. His father's name is Zheng Hai and he makes a living pulling a rickshaw. His mother works in a yarn factory. The boy is wearing an old hat from Shanghai North Public School, a black striped cotton-padded jacket, black striped trousers, one black cloth shoe, and one yellow leather shoe. He has now been transferred to the Women and Children's Relief Association for care and collection.

Yesterday's Robbery

Rue Bayle. Yesterday at around 8:00 AM, five robbers suddenly came to the home of Gu Shunsheng, a local resident at No. 28, Chengqing Lane, Rue Bayle, in the French Concession. Under the pretext of renting a house, they entered through the back door. Each held a handgun and forced all the adults and children in the house into the back parlor, warning them not to make a sound. One robber stood guard at the door with a gun, while the other four searched the downstairs, taking valuables. After about twenty minutes, they each fled with their loot. They stole clothing, gold jewelry, and silver dollars, totaling approximately 1,250 yuan. The victim filed a loss report with the Songshan Road Police Station requesting an investigation.

News from Various Labor Unions

Hua Sheng Electrical Workers Union. Declaration in support of the Commerce Press Workers Union's protest against the assault by French sailors (excerpt above). Compatriots, you must understand that this assault is not just about the injuries of a few individuals. Our four hundred million compatriots are constantly at risk of being stabbed anywhere. Regarding this incident, we will certainly demand that they punish the perpetrators, apologize, and take responsibility for compensating the losses. At the same time, we absolutely cannot allow similar incidents to happen again within our complete territory. We must reclaim foreign concessions, abolish unequal treaties, and strive to achieve this in the shortest possible time. In order to safeguard national sovereignty and protect the peace of our compatriots, we vow to be the backing force and fight together. This is our declaration.

Southern Goods Workers Union. The Zhi Sheng, Yu Kang, Shun Chang Qian, Chang Yu, Tai Sheng Run, and Fifth Group held a joint meeting the night before last. Ling Baode was publicly elected as chairman and the meeting proceeded with due formalities. The chairman first reported the purpose of the meeting to break the deadlock. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Regarding the working hours, it was resolved that work hours will be from 7:00 AM to 7:30 PM, a unified shift system, to be implemented from April 6. (2) Regarding whether to re-elect the investigators, it was resolved to re-elect all of them. Zhi Sheng: Yao Jinbao; Shun Chang Qian: Lu Boshun; Yu Kang: Cai Liansheng; Tai Sheng Run: Fan Nianci; Chang Yu: Zheng Rongsheng. (3) Regarding the investigation method, it was resolved that they will take turns on duty, with each person working six days per month. Work will be evidenced by stamped records. Chang Yu: first term; Zhi Sheng: second term; Shun Chang Qian: third term; Yu Kang: fourth term; Tai Sheng Run: fifth term. (4) Regarding the clock standardization, it was resolved that the clock in the store where the investigator is on duty will be the standard. (5) Regarding investigators' absence due to official business, it was resolved that the group leader will act as an agent. (6) Regarding how to handle violations of working hours, it was resolved that the first offense will be a warning, the second offense will be a fine of one dollar, and the third offense will result in the cancellation of public record rights for three months. Temporary motions: (1) Regarding the method of paying monthly dues for Zhi Sheng and Shun Chang Qian, it was resolved that payment will be made monthly from the public record and paid according to the receipt when public dividends are issued. (2) Regarding who is responsible for keeping the public record book, it was resolved that the group leader will be responsible for safekeeping. (3) Regarding the method of paying monthly rent for Tai Sheng Run, it was resolved that the group leader will be responsible for submitting the payment when monthly regulations are issued on the 16th of each month. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

How to Commemorate "April 12th"?

Eliminate the remnants of the Chinese Communist Party

Overthrow the Northern Warlord Yan Xishan

Abolish all unequal treaties Support Chairman Chiang, who has contributed greatly to the hard work

(1) The April 12th Party Purification Commemoration is the anniversary of our party's elimination of Communist Party members who had joined our party. It is a crucial turning point for our party, a matter of great importance to the people's welfare, the foundation of the nation, and the safety of the nation. We should use this opportunity to conduct large-scale propaganda for purging the party and opposing communism in order to eradicate the roots of the Communist Party and consolidate the foundation of our party.

(2) The purpose of the propaganda for purging the party and opposing communism can be explained from two aspects: purging the party and opposing communism. The so-called propaganda for purging the party is to make the public understand the intentions, process, and relationships of our party's purging of party members who had joined our party. Make the public understand that if the party members who had joined our party are not eliminated, then the party will not be the party, and the country will not be the country. The so-called anti-communist propaganda is to make the public understand the crimes of the Communist Party, not only should they not be allowed to live in our party, but they should also be prevented from acting and their followers should be wiped out.

(3) Our party's tolerance of the Communist Party in the thirteenth year was to tolerate individual Communist Party members in the hope that they would be loyal to the Three Principles of the People, not to tolerate the entire Communist Party in order to divide the Kuomintang. Unexpectedly, after the Communist Party members who hung a sheep's head to sell dog meat joined the Kuomintang, they acted in the name of the Kuomintang and practiced the Communist Party's reality, distorting the Three Principles of the People, confusing young people, and forcing workers to be their sacrificial tools. They used all kinds of methods to try to steal party power and seize power in order to achieve their goal of "China returning to Russia."

(4) At the critical moment of the Northern Expedition in the sixteenth year, the Communist Party used methods of profit inducement and coercion to instigate workers and friends to strike without cause, causing disturbances in various places to disrupt the rear of the Northern Expedition. On the one hand, they used the means of instigation and alienation to isolate the united front of our party and the revolutionary people from all walks of life, so as to eliminate their sympathy for the party. It can be said that they have exhausted the ability of sinister destruction, and their only attempt is to destroy the National Revolution in order to subvert our party and destroy China. Fortunately, the advanced comrades of our party extracted their conspiracy and resolutely decided to carry out the purification of the party on April 12 of the sixteenth year and eliminate all the party members who had joined our party. Therefore, the party purification movement is our party's primary task of saving the party, and it is also the only way to save the country, because our party is purging the party in order to eliminate the obstacles to "China's independence," to complete the mission of our party in order to "consolidate the foundation of our party," and to protect the interests of the people to purge the party.

(5) The work of purifying the party is certainly important, but purifying the party is only one of the methods of anti-communism, not the only method of anti-communism. If the party is only purified without continuing to oppose communism, then the remaining forces of communism will not be easily eliminated, and it is difficult to guarantee that they will not revive. Therefore, after purifying the party, we must continue to oppose communism and fundamentally eliminate the Chinese Communist Party.

(6) Passive anti-communist work is certainly necessary, but the construction work on the positive side is also very important. The people should support our party's training of the people to the point, and assist the government in engaging in construction, implementing local autonomy, and completing the work of training the government. This can be said to be positive anti-communist work.

(7) Finally, we must have a deep understanding that our party has resolutely eliminated the Communist Party in the past period, then the reactionary elements in the future, such as the reorganization faction, the West Mountain Conference faction, all expelled party ruffians, and unscrupulous politicians, and the Northern Warlords with feudal ideas, who do not understand China's environment, and are confused about the general trend of the world, slander the central government, and deliberately sabotage, often suffer from the Communist Party's utilization without knowing it themselves. As far away as Feng Tang, Zhang Li's arbitrary declaration of soldiers, and as close as Yan Xishan's betrayal of the party and the country, they are not tolerated by our party, and they are especially included in the ranks of absolute elimination and eradication. Therefore, before the anti-revolutionary elements have not been eliminated for a day, the National Revolution led by our party cannot succeed for a day. Comrades of our party should be diligent and courageous, and make extra efforts to realize the doctrines of the whole party as soon as possible and make the revolution a success as soon as possible. This is really the point that we should pay attention to and work hard for in the future.

(8) Slogans: 1. Eliminate the Chinese Communist Party 2. Consolidate the foundation of our party 3. Consolidate the regime of our party 4. Eliminate all reactionary forces 5. Overthrow the Northern Warlord Yan Xishan 6. Unify the will of the Three Principles of the People 7. Strive for training and construction 8. Abolish all unequal treaties 9. Long live the Chinese Kuomintang 10. Long live the Republic of China

Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Cloudy along the coast of Shandong with northwest winds. Mostly cloudy skies with gentle southeast breezes in this area and the Yangtze River basin. Northeast winds and occasional light fog along the coast south of Ma'an Island. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 71.6 degrees and the lowest was 47.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 68.0 degrees and the lowest was 53.6 degrees.

Market News

Recently, book industry colleagues have united major bookstores such as Datong, Xinhua, Qunxue, Shishi, Datong, and Youzheng to organize a joint grand discount sale market for new and old books on the second floor of the former site of the Shishi Daily News at the corner of Simalu and Wangping Street. Preparations are now complete and the opening is scheduled for April 11th. Bookstores interested in joining can contact the market office.

Recently, the equipment has been completed and the opening date is not far away. At that time, there will also be a grand sale.

Social News Submission Guidelines

(1) The text is limited to news about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, rural areas, health, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life.

(2) The pictures are limited to lyrical paintings related to social life.

(3) Photos of seasonal scenery, plants, people, and news photography are qualified. Seasonal scenery photography, especially with ladies, is especially welcome.

(4) The number of words in each article should not exceed 2,000 at most.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the paper.

(6) Do not write horizontally, do not write carelessly, and save western characters as much as possible. If you have to use the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not draw pictures with blue ink or use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate that the submission should be sent to the Social News Department.

(9) Whether the submission is published or not, it will not be returned. If you need to return it, please state it in advance and attach sufficient postage stamps.
